Generalissimo Chiang Kai-shek Inspects Troops in Hunan 96

Famous National Martial Arts Masters from North and South Perform Martial Arts

Chiang Delivers Earnest Admonitions to All Soldiers

After the Inspection, He Travels to Mount Heng to Visit the Southern Peak

Changsha Correspondence: Yesterday (the 1st) at 6:30 AM, Generalissimo Chiang Kai-shek, together with He Jian, toured scenic spots on Mount Yuelu, including the Yu Wang Stele and Baihe Spring. At 9:00 AM, they descended the mountain, crossed the river, and returned to the provincial capital, proceeding to Jingwu Gate and the outer training grounds to inspect the Fourth Route Army troops stationed in the province. The details are as follows:

He Jian had previously designated Li Jue, commander of the 19th Division, as the temporary commander for the troop inspection and tasked him with preparatory matters. The troops inspected included: (1) the 112th Regiment and artillery battalion of the 19th Division, (2) the 1st Garrison Regiment, (3) the Training Corps, (4) the Technical Training Brigade, (5) the infantry and artillery company of the 28th Army, (6) the National Martial Arts Training Institute, and (7) an aviation demonstration.

Attendees: Before 9:00 AM, those arriving at the scene included Liu Jianxu, commander of the 28th Army; Peng Songling, chief of staff; Wang Dongyuan, commander of the 15th Division; Chen Kongda, chief of staff; Peng Renren, commander of the 16th Division; Guo Chiping, deputy commander; Yang Shisong, chief of staff; Li Jue, commander of the 19th Division; Luo Shujia, deputy commander; Huang Sufu, chief of staff; Tao Guang, commander of the 62nd Division; Zhou Xiwu, deputy commander; Zhang Dingwan, chief of staff; Chen Guangzhong, commander of the 63rd Division; Hu Da, provincial capital garrison commander; Liu Yinggu, chief of staff of the Fourth Route Army Headquarters; Xiong Shiding, adjutant general; Cao Bowen, head of the Department of Civil Affairs; Zhang Kailian, head of the Department of Finance; Tan Changkai, head of the Department of Construction; and over 300 personnel above section chief level from party, government, and military agencies. Inspection Circumstances: The troops to be inspected arrived at the scene at 7:00 AM. At 9:30 AM, Generalissimo Chiang Kai-shek, accompanied by He Jian, arrived at the scene. Amidst the melodious military music, they ascended the inspection platform, and the inspection commenced. Under the command of Li Jue, all officers and soldiers first circled the grounds once and paid their highest respects to Chiang. This was followed by a marching review and a demonstration of close-order drill by the companies. The officers and soldiers demonstrated precise footwork, which was highly praised by Chiang. Next, the Technical Brigade demonstrated group exercises, including five items: linked fists, basic fists, Tongbei Fist, splitting knife, and bayonet thrusting. Subsequently, the National Martial Arts Training Institute performed group calisthenics, which were all impressive. At the same time, the Aviation Office dispatched three aircraft, which circled the sky, flying around the inspection grounds ten times, sometimes together, sometimes dispersed, sometimes high, sometimes low, and also performed aerial combat.

Performing National Martial Arts: At approximately 11:00 AM, after the troop inspection was completed, instructors from both the Technical Training Brigade and the National Martial Arts Training Institute demonstrated national martial arts. The instructors were all famous masters from various schools of both the North and the South. The order of performance was as follows: (1) Li Zhengchang (age 80), Monkey Fist; (2) Shen Jingming (age 13), Gongli Fist; (3) Zhang Boda, Shaolin Fist; (4) Gong Youcai, Changquan; (5) Guo Xian’san, Taijiquan; (6) Fan Houxi, Shaolin Staff; (7) Li Shunan, Single Saber; (8) Zhang Xiangwu, Wudang Sword; (9) Zhao Ronglin, Pigua Palm; (10) Wang Zhihe, Chaquan; (11) Xin Jianhou, Xingyiquan; (12) Lin Cunyuan, Tongbei Fist; (13) Wang Chengzhang, Single Saber; (14) Li Fuchun, Yang Family Spear; (15) Shi Hanzhang, Guandao; (16) Yan Fengying (female instructor), Qingping Sword; (17) Yan Fenglin, Ditang Saber; (18) Zhu Guozhen, Drunken Eight Immortals; (19) Gu Ruzhang, Cannon Fist; (20) Zhu Guolu, Green Steel Sword; (21) Liu Changkui and Gong Youcai, sparring fist; (22) Zhang Xiangwu and Yan Fenglin, paired swordplay; (23) Zhu Guozhen and Shi Hanzhang, double broadswords against spear; (24) Yan Fengying and Yan Fenglin, unarmed against fork; (25) Zhu Rong and Li Fuchun, unarmed knife disarm; (26) Xu Ruiying and Zhao Ronglin, broadsword against spear; (27) Yan Fengying and Yan Fenglin, double sabers against spear; (28) Shi Hanzhang and Zhu Guozhen, paired broadswords; (29) grappling. Finally, Li Liji, captain of the Technical Brigade and a famous Taiji master, performed Taiji sword. Generalissimo Chiang Kai-shek greatly praised the performance and especially commended the young instructor Shen Jingming and the female instructor Yan Fengying.

Chiang's Admonition: After the martial arts performance, Generalissimo Chiang Kai-shek ordered the officers and soldiers present to assemble in front of the stage for an address. He stated, in essence, that the violent Japanese had forcibly occupied our Northeast Three Provinces, and the country was now at a critical juncture of survival. In the past, the people of Hunan, such as Zeng, Zuo, Huang, and Cai, had all made significant and earth-shattering contributions to saving China from danger, earning the respect of the entire country. The Fourth Route Army, under the leadership of Commander-in-Chief He, was composed of Hunanese. At this time of national crisis, it was hoped that they would carry forward the spirit of the Hunanese of the past, defeat Japanese imperialism, and save China from danger. Having just witnessed the martial arts performance, we should understand that the reason martial arts can be effective in combat is because of the speed and precision of the movements. The same principle applies to the military in order to win battles. It is hoped that the Fourth Route Army, as the armed force of the people, will ensure that every movement is swift and precise, becoming a national model army.

The Troops Cheer: After Chiang's address, the officers and soldiers present were energized and cheered in support of Generalissimo Chiang Kai-shek's efforts to resist Japan and suppress bandits, shouting slogans such as "Long live Generalissimo Chiang Kai-shek!", "Long live the Chinese Kuomintang!", and "Long live the Republic of China!" The meeting was then adjourned.

After the adjournment, Generalissimo Chiang Kai-shek, accompanied by his wife, traveled by car from the province to Mount Heng at 12:00 PM. He Jian and his wife, as well as Liu Jianxu, Chen Cheng, Wang Dongyuan, Li Jue,

Chen Guangzhong, Tao Guang, Peng Zairen, members of the Provincial Party Headquarters and the Provincial Government, and prominent figures from all walks of life, also followed in approximately 20 cars. They were expected to arrive at Mount Heng around 6:00 PM and planned to spend three days touring the mountain. They would descend the mountain on the fourth day. Tents were brought by plane from Lushan, and Chiang and Song planned to camp overnight at Zhurong Peak on Mount Heng in order to watch the sunrise the following morning. (November 2nd)

Anhui Rice Merchants Oppose Excessive Taxes 97

Wuhu Correspondence: The Anhui Provincial Government has specially established a Rice and Grain Management Bureau to collect a rice export tax of 6 jiao per dan. The people of Anhui have already risen up in opposition. Recently, the Wuhu Business Tax Office, citing Article 5 of the revised Business Tax Regulations of the province, decided to order all rice firms to withhold 0.4% of the business tax from merchants starting October 1st, with the office sending personnel to collect it daily. The rice merchants had strongly protested the levying of business tax on rice and grain last year, but the issue was not resolved. Now, it has suddenly been increased threefold (the original tax last year was set at 0.1%), which is difficult to accept. Moreover, the price of rice in Anhui Province this year is lower than in other provinces, which is due to the excessive tax collection by the provincial government. Now, without regard for the people's hardship, it arbitrarily imposes heavy taxes, directly collecting them from merchants and indirectly from the people. At a time when the entire

Page 11

Important News 98

Country knows that cheap grain hurts farmers and is jointly planning relief measures, the authorities in this province are instead increasing taxes on rice and grain, hindering its circulation, which is tantamount to abandoning farmers. In addition to notifying the rice industry associations of Guang, Chao, Yan, and Ning to work together to fight for relief, today they also wired the Provincial Federation of Chambers of Commerce, requesting that it immediately forward the message to the Anhui Provincial Government and the Business Tax Bureau, as well as the Rice and Grain Export Management Committee, to abolish the excessive taxes in order to alleviate the suffering of merchants. (November 2nd)

Bengbu Huai Salt Competitive Operation Dispute 99

Transportation Merchants Establish North Salt Public Business Office

Salt Firms Fear Loss of Livelihood and Vigorously Oppose

Bengbu Correspondence: Northern Anhui is a distribution area for Huai salt, traditionally managed by merchants for transportation and sale, unlike the salt transportation system in southern Anhui, which allows for free trading. Since the development of salt transportation by train in Bengbu, all industries have flourished, and the number of salt firms has increased to 57. These salt firms all hold long-term (ten-year) salt brokerage licenses issued by the Department of Finance, acting as intermediaries, collecting a commission of 1 jiao 9 fen per dan (the firms actually receive 9 fen, with the remainder going to local surtaxes and the salt industry association). Recently, the Huaibei Salt Affairs Inspection Sub-office suddenly issued a notice stating that Bengbu Huai salt was being sold at discounted prices, causing great instability. The main reason was the manipulative practices that led to significant disputes, which required strict measures to stabilize salt administration. Subsequently, the sale of salt in Bengbu should be managed by transportation merchants who would display salt samples for public viewing and purchase, with all salt firms treated as ordinary buyers, unable to force transportation merchants or households to trade on their behalf, to prevent corruption. At the same time, transportation merchants such as Zhang Xian'gen established the North Salt Public Business Office in Furunli to assess salt quality and set prices, declaring that no commissions would be charged, resembling the former Huai Salt Price Stabilization Bureau. As a result, the 57 salt firms became greatly alarmed, believing that this move by the transportation merchants would deprive them of their livelihoods, and they opposed it fiercely. The Salt Industry Association convened an emergency meeting of representatives from all salt firms on the afternoon of the 1st, resolving to send Yang Yaonan and others to Beijing to petition. Today (the 3rd), they gathered salt industry workers and related labor groups, holding a large-scale demonstration. At 10:00 AM, they gathered at the Transportation Association, with about 3,000 participants, marching and shouting slogans such as "Abolish the North Salt Public Business Office," heading to the Fourth Division Headquarters, Fengyang County Government, Bengbu Garrison Headquarters, Changhuai Water Police Bureau, Bengbu District Party Headquarters, and the Huaibei Inspection Sub-office's tax collection office to petition. They dispersed around 2:00 PM. This dispute is unlikely to be resolved soon. (November 3rd)

Zhang Hanying Discusses His Impressions of Inspecting the Yellow River 100

Jinan Correspondence: The Ministry of Interior's Water Conservancy Commission specially appointed Wang Yingyu to inspect the entire Yellow River to plan a comprehensive governance strategy. Wang arrived in Jinan in the middle of last month, first inspecting the lower reaches of the Yellow River's entry into the sea at Lijin. After returning to Jinan, he went to the upper reaches for inspection. Zhang Lianjia, director of the River Affairs Bureau, specially assigned the engineering section chief Pan Fen to accompany him. Zhang Hanying, president of the Jinan Engineering Society, also accompanied them. Zhang Hanying has now returned to Jinan. I asked him about the itinerary along the river. Zhang said that a month ago, they departed from Jinan, first arriving at Shilibu, and then went upstream the next day, entering Puyang and Dongming in Hebei Province, passing through Kaocheng and arriving in Kaifeng, Henan. On the second day in Kaifeng, they inspected the Jialu River in Zhuxian Town, because the river is also a tributary of the Yellow River and had been recently dredged and repaired by the Henan Provincial Government. They inspected it in great detail. On the third day, they went to Chenqiao, north of Kaifeng, to inspect a section of alkaline land, about five or six li from north to south and over twenty li from northeast, unsuitable for planting. Recently, the Henan Provincial Government planned to divert Yellow River water to silt it up in order to encourage people to cultivate it. Wang Committee member (Yingyu) deeply approved of the proposal. From there, they went upstream to Wuzhi County and Meng County. They originally planned to go to Gong County, but because it was difficult to travel by car, they changed to a train and went to Luoyang first, inspecting the Luo River in Luoyang. The river's irrigation capacity is very large, benefiting many farmlands. However, the Luo River is lower than the Yellow River, and when the water is high, it cannot discharge into the Yellow River, often causing backflow and flooding. This is one problem. Luoyang has the Beimang Mountains, where the tomb of Emperor Guangwu of Han is located. The Yellow River passes under the mountain, eroding the roots of the mountain, and soil blocks often collapse. Ships do not dare to approach. The Yellow River carries sediment, which is another major cause. From Luoyang to Mengjin, according to the locals, the Yellow River has shifted more than twenty li southward in recent years. From there, they returned to Gong County to inspect the Yi River. The advantages and disadvantages of this water are the same as those of the Luo River. At this point, I returned to Jinan, while Wang Committee member continued westward, planning to enter Gansu via Shaanxi, to see the Wushu Mountains, and to reach Qinghai to explore the source of the Yellow River. Then, he planned to go to Hetao and then return to Shandong to visit Chiang Kai-shek in Hankou. Because Chiang had said that as long as there was a way to manage the Yellow River, funding would not be a problem, Wang Yingyu planned to report on the inspection of the entire river and offer suggestions for governing the Yellow River. According to our opinion, governing the Yellow River is by no means as difficult as imagined. Wang Yingyu's opinion, in summary, can be divided into three points: (1) Dredge the end of the Yellow River into the sea to facilitate discharge. (2) The riverbed within Henan Province is too wide, up to forty or fifty li in some places, making it almost impossible to find its true channel. Therefore, the six major changes of the Yellow River have all occurred above Shandong, below Zhengzhou. Efforts should be made to narrow it slightly. (3) Dig the Wushu Mountains to prevent the Tao River from flowing into the Yellow River and instead flow into the Wei River, and then into the Yellow River through the Wei River. This approach can reduce the water volume in Hetao. Once the water is reduced, the sediment carried will also be reduced. After the Tao River enters the Wei River, the increase in clear water will flow into the Yellow River, which can flush away sediment. As far as we know, there are three sources of sediment in the Yellow River: Ningxia, Hetao, and the North Mountain. If we can reduce the water volume in Hetao and build stone dams throughout the river (because after consulting locals along the river in Shandong and Henan, it was said that there were no breaches in places with stone dams), we believe that the Yellow River flood could be permanently eliminated. Although building stone dams is more expensive, it can be done once and for all. Wang Yingyu also suggested that water should be diverted from many places to reduce Yellow River flooding. We originally planned to set up reservoirs along the river to regulate the Yellow River's water flow, but we did not see any suitable locations from Shandong to Henan. I asked Wang to look for a reservoir location further upstream. The above is just a small opinion after our inspection of the Yellow River, not a plan. In the future, it will still need to be carefully studied by national water conservancy experts. (November 3rd)

Songjiang 101

Xia Family in Xinqiao Robbed: At approximately 1:00 AM on the 1st, three bandits suddenly broke into the home of Xia Xiaodi in the 16th Jia of the 10th Sub-station of Xinqiao. The victim was awakened from his sleep and saw three uninvited guests wearing short, multi-colored clothes, speaking in Hakka dialect, and holding wooden clubs. They violently tied up the victim and forced him to reveal where he had hidden his silver. The victim suffered a shoulder injury. The bandits then rummaged through chests and cabinets, looting money and clothing. Neighbor Xia Wenxiang shouted, causing the bandits to flee with their loot. Xia Wenxiang chased after them but was attacked by the bandits and suffered facial injuries. He pursued them to Inada, where he managed to apprehend one of the bandits, who identified himself as Zheng Zisheng from Zhenjiang. He was immediately sent to the 10th Sub-station and then transferred to the main station for investigation.

Kunshan 102

Two Families Robbed in Zhou Shu's Taiping River Area: Zhu Zhaokun, a farmer in Taiping River Village, Zhou Shu Township, was invaded by bandits speaking with a northern accent the night before last. The bandits forbade the family from making any noise and robbed them of silver and jewelry. They then went to the home of Wu Wenkui in the same village and stole clothing and silver worth over a hundred yuan.

A Ferry Boat Robbed Mid-Journey: A ferry boat traveling between Kunshan and Shatou was attacked by robbers on the 2nd. The boat departed from Shatou for Kunshan, carrying more than a dozen passengers. When the boat reached Genglou Bridge in this county, multiple robbers with guns ordered the boat to stop. The boatman had no choice but to dock the boat. The bandits boarded the boat and searched it, and they left with their loot after half an hour. After checking, the passengers had been robbed of over a hundred yuan in silver and a large amount of goods. On the 3rd, the boatman reported the incident to the Kunshan Public Security Bureau. Director Qin reportedly ordered the detective team to investigate and apprehend the fleeing robbers.

Taicang 103

Shanghai Anti-Traitor Group Warns Traitorous Merchants: Department stores, foreign goods stores, and general merchandise stores in the cities and towns of this county are holding autumn sales. The other day, the Tonghexiang Silk and Cloth Store in Penglai Town ordered a large number of enemy goods from Shanghai. The Shanghai Blood Soul Anti-Traitor Group detected this and sent a letter of warning yesterday. The letter stated that the store was making every effort to promote Japanese goods during the sale, and they warned the store to seal up the inferior goods or they would take severe measures. They also asked the store to inform all sale merchants to seal up all Japanese goods.

A Miracle of Triplets: Li Jinlin, wife of Zhou Fengliang, owner of the Zhoulong Coal Store on South Street in the city, had been pregnant for ten months. Her abdomen was larger than usual. She gave birth last night and delivered triplets, all boys. Mother and children are all healthy, which is truly rare.

Wuxi 104

Telegraph Order to Report on Grain Reserves: Since 1922, Wuxi has not levied grain reserves due to severe financial difficulties. All previous reserves were diverted and used during previous price equalization efforts. By last year, there were only about 20,000 yuan left. This summer, the disaster in the villages was very serious, and this money was used to allocate the worst-hit areas for relief. Now there is nothing left. Public groups have repeatedly wired the provincial government, requesting that they continue to levy grain reserve funds, but this has not been approved. Later, the provincial government stated that this autumn harvest was abundant, and all counties' charity granaries should implement grain reserves. The Department of Civil Affairs formulated five provisional measures for building granaries and accumulating grain, ordering all counties to strictly comply. The county government reported the past grain reserve experience of Wuxi to the provincial government. Yesterday, the provincial government sent a telegraph order that it was now the time for the autumn harvest, and they should urgently raise funds to handle grain reserves to maintain the people's food supply. They asked how Wuxi had progressed and ordered them to provide a detailed report as soon as possible for assessment.

The Reaction to Refining Sandalwood Oil: Near the Tiantang Catholic Church in Beitang Sanliqiao, Zhang Zhongnan of Hengchang Ironworks recently set up a sandalwood oil kerosene factory, refining kerosene by machine every day. Peng Xiwen, director of the 5th Public Security Bureau, because the factory was located in a busy city and was likely to cause danger, reported to the main bureau for instructions and ordered it to be banned. However, the factory ignored the law and continued refining as usual. The neighbors nearby have risen up in opposition and jointly submitted a letter to the county government and public security bureau yesterday, requesting that police be sent to stop it to protect life and property, and asking that the person in charge of the factory be summoned for investigation.

Changzhou 105

Villagers Destroy District Office: The 19th District Office of Wuyi is located in the Dongyue Temple in Wansui Town. Recently, some villagers initiated a celebration for welcoming the gods. Xie Yingzheng, the district chief, because the rural economy was declining and the local area was uneasy, gathered the heads of the celebration to persuade them to stop it. On the 27th and 28th of last month, reactionary notices suddenly appeared in the town, declaring that the district office must be overthrown. Xie District Chief, seeing the situation was not good, requested the county government to send police to the town to maintain order. On the evening of the 2nd of this month, at about 5:00 PM, most of the villagers suddenly rang gongs and gathered a crowd, bringing flammable materials with them, breaking down the gate of the district office and rushing in. They threw bricks and stones and destroyed the office, burning all equipment and documents. At that time, the police team was unable to stop them due to being outnumbered. In a crisis, Xie District Chief jumped out of the building with the official seal and escaped with his life. Some staff members are missing. After escaping, Xie District Chief came to the city overnight to report to the county government and requested assistance from various agencies. The county government ordered You Zhenji, the public security chief of the town, to investigate and arrest the instigators.

Changshu 106

Joint Salary Demand Meeting of Two District Schools: The education funding in this county has been in arrears for many years, now reaching seven or eight months. Those responsible for education have not been able to come up with a good solution, causing unease among those serving in education. The last year's arrears totaled more than six months. Although school has been in session for a long time this year, the bureau has only paid for two and a half months as a formality. The schools are unable to maintain themselves, and the situation in the countryside is even worse. Now that the 21st area's taxes have begun to be levied, the education funding being collected totals more than 400,000 yuan, but the authorities are still not releasing it. The schools are therefore extremely panicked. The other day, the 4th school district held a salary demand meeting for the teachers and staff of each school in Bixi City. They unanimously decided to petition the education bureau to be responsible for repaying half of the old debt in the shortest possible time, and the new funds must not be delayed again. The schools in the 3rd school district are also taking similar action and are said to be joining together to petition the city this week.

Pinghu 109

A Tragically Disabled Monk by Gambling Thugs: Dai Li, the principal of a certain elementary school in the city, left his wife and children impoverished after his death. His wife was blind, so she sold her son to the North Temple to become a monk in order to pay for the funeral. She herself worked as a peddler, which she had been doing for years. The other day, gamblers were gathering to gamble in the North Temple when they were discovered by the Public Security Bureau, who arrested the gambler Zhang and punished him. Zhang suspected that Dai's son had reported him. After being released, he and several other gamblers lured Dai's son to their house. Zhang and his wife tied up Dai's son and beat him repeatedly. They then used two yellow croaker tail needles to nail into his knees. This needle is the most poisonous, causing the flesh to rot without healing. Many local ruffians hoard them for revenge. Immediately, Dai's son shouted for help, but Zhang's wife sprinkled quicklime into his eyes, immediately blinding and muting him, and he fainted to the ground. The next day, someone discovered him, covered in blood and barely alive, so they sent him to the hospital. Today, a needle has been removed. The doctor said that both legs must be amputated to save his life. The perpetrators have all fled.

Kuomintang Member Arrested for Conspiring with Bandits: Gan Kaijun, the captain of the county's basic team, captured Cai Shen, the leader of the false "Number One Army in the World," and Wang Yahua, a female student from Songjiang, and other accomplices. This has been reported in the newspaper. It has now been discovered that a certain Huang, a party member of the 4th District, has evidence of conspiracy with bandits. He had sneaked in from Shanghai and was watching a play at the Xinmin Theater. The police calmly arrested him on the spot and sent him to the county government, where he was shackled and detained with Cai Shen and others to await interrogation.

Hangzhou 110

Lin Min Acquitted in the Xu Zhuoran Murder Case: The case of Xu Zhuoran, a prominent Fujian Min party figure, being stabbed to death in Xiamen was transferred to the Hangzhou County Local Court in 1930. After repeated trials, in June 1931, the court acquitted the three suspects of conspiracy to murder, Ye Cai-Zhen, Chen Yan-Xiang, and Chen De-Lin. However, Lin Luo was sentenced to four years in prison for possessing military weapons. The prosecutor appealed to the High Court, and the case was under appeal. Later, the troops stationed in Fujian Province captured Lin Min, the main suspect in this case, and the suspects Chen Chang, and the witnesses Zhang Jichang and Liu Zhi, and sent them to Hangzhou for investigation. It was deemed that there was insufficient evidence, and Chen Chang, Zhang Jichang, and Liu Zhi were declared not prosecuted. As for the suspect Lin Min, the Hangzhou County Local Court opened a trial on October 28th. Lin not only denied killing Xu, but also denied that he was Yao Min, claiming that his real name was Zhang Meng. After debate by the lawyers on both sides, the judge declared the debate in this case concluded. Yesterday (the 4th) afternoon at 2:00 PM, the verdict was announced. Judge Zhu Bao-Ren summoned Lin Min, asked about his age and origin. Lin still claimed that his real name was Zhang Meng, not Lin Min. The judge declared: (1) Lin Min is definitely Lin Min, not Zhang Meng. (2) There is insufficient evidence to prove that Lin Min committed the murder, so he is declared not guilty. The ancillary civil lawsuit filed by Xu's wife, Ye, was rejected.

Taizhou 111

A Fatal Shooting in Daiheng: A farmer named Tang Zhixiang from Daiheng, Tiantai, was on his way home from Baohua Temple in his village early the other morning. As he passed the temple entrance, he was suddenly shot dead with a handgun. The family reported the case to the local authorities for investigation, but it is unknown whether the perpetrator will be apprehended.

A Major Fire in Dazi Lane: Dazi Lane, located inside the North Gate of Huangyan, is home to hundreds of shops, a thriving business district, and the heart of the city. On the morning of the 28th of this month at 1:00 AM, a sudden fire broke out, engulfing more than 300 shops. Fire brigades from various districts rushed to the scene and worked tirelessly to extinguish the blaze, which took seven hours. It is said that the losses are incalculable.

Correspondence 112

Letter from Zhu Jingzhi of Taicang: Respectfully, I have just read in your esteemed newspaper's local correspondence column on the 1st of this month that Taicang County will implement a public opium sale, and that the various townships of Shaxi are contracted by Zhu Jingzhi, etc. I was shocked upon reading this. The scourge of opium is known to all. I have been in the business community for more than twenty years, and I have recently been entrusted with the position of sixth district commander of the county's defense corps. I ask myself daily about local public affairs. I have never heard of the public sale of opium in this county. As for the claim that I have contracted it, it is even further from the truth. I believe it is a mistake due to inaccurate reporting by the interviewer. This matter concerns my reputation, and I am writing this letter specifically to correct the record. I request that it be published in the correspondence column to rectify the mishearing and clarify the facts. I respectfully send this to the esteemed chief editor of the Shen Bao. Respectfully, Zhu Jingzhi, November 3rd.

Important News

The Issue of the Minister of Education After Weng Wenhao's Resignation 113

Zhu Jiahua Urges Weng to Come to Beijing by Telegram

There is Talk of Duan Xipeng Temporarily Acting as Minister

Zhu Jiahua Urges Weng by Telegram: Zhu Jiahua, the Minister of Transportation, arrived on the 3rd to take office. However, Weng Wenhao, the Minister of Education, has repeatedly expressed his refusal to take the position. Former Minister of Education Zhu Jiahua, knowing that he must go to the Ministry of Transportation to oversee matters and that the Ministry of Education's responsibilities are important and cannot be left without leadership, sent a telegram to the new Minister of Education, Weng Wenhao, in Beijing on the 3rd, urging him to come to Beijing immediately to take office. The telegram stated roughly: "I have been repeatedly urged to go to the Ministry of Transportation and have decided to go to Jiang on the (3rd) to take office. The affairs of the Ministry of Education are important and cannot be left without leadership. Please come to Beijing quickly to take office." After Zhu went to the Ministry of Transportation, he temporarily entrusted the affairs of the Ministry of Education to the two vice ministers to handle until the new minister arrives, at which point he will formally hand over the duties.

Weng's Resignation Issue: Since the Central Government appointed Weng as the Minister of Education, Weng, who was in Beijing at the time, immediately stated that he had not been consulted beforehand and was unwilling to take the position. When Weng went to Beijing, he also told reporters that he was firmly resigning from the Ministry of Education. The Executive Yuan has sent a telegram of consolation, urging him to come to Beijing to take office quickly. As of the 3rd, they had not yet received Weng's reply. Therefore, although there has been much speculation in society about the successor to Weng after his resignation, these are all just groundless rumors. The government has not yet formally discussed the matter. Talk of Duan Xipeng Acting as Minister: Since the Central Government announced Weng as the Minister of Education, the Vice Minister of Education, Duan Xipeng, immediately claimed illness and resigned. However, after being consoled by the Executive Yuan, he resumed his duties at the Ministry of Education on the 2nd. As a result, there is a strong rumor that the Third Plenary Session of the Central Executive Committee is approaching. If Weng Wenhao is truly determined to resign, Duan will temporarily act as Minister, and a formal appointment will be made after the Third Plenary Session of the Central Executive Committee. This rumor seems plausible, and we will record it here for verification.

Zhu Jiahua Cables Zhejiang to Demand 20,000 Yuan in Foil Tax for Education 114

The Jiang-Zhe foil and business tax has an annual revenue of 2.7 million yuan, with a monthly revenue of over 200,000 yuan. After consultation between the Jiang-Zhe provinces, in addition to supplementing the Ministry of Education's expenses with 10,000 yuan per month, 22,500 yuan will be allocated to the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education and Finance. The remaining revenue will belong to Zhejiang Province. Due to financial difficulties, various provinces are significantly in arrears on payments to the Ministry. A few days ago, Zhou Junyan, Director of the Zhejiang Department of Finance, returned to Hangzhou from Hankou. When he passed through Nanjing, Minister Zhu Jiahua had personally discussed and approved the immediate remittance of 40,000 yuan. Now that Zhu has been ordered to transfer to the Ministry of Transportation and has already handed over his duties, he specifically sent a telegram to Zhou yesterday, saying that he had promised to plan to supplement the Ministry's education funds with 40,000 yuan. Although the Ministry of Education will soon be handing over its duties and cannot clear the education expenses, the items for the education funds must be further divided. Please allocate 20,000 yuan to be remitted to Beijing within the next few days to meet urgent needs.

Ministry of Education Changes the Organization of Beijing Normal University 115

Beijing, 4th: Since news of the Ministry of Education's plan to change the organization of Normal University spread, the education community in Beijing has paid close attention. It is said that this is the Ministry of Education's change to the entire national education plan. The methods are: 1. Establish high-level normal school classes in ordinary universities; 2. Normal University recruits graduates from ordinary universities and provides them with one or two years of normal training; 3. Vocational education teachers will be recruited through examinations.

Local News

The International Education Society Was Established Yesterday 117

▲ Kangpu Was Elected President

▲ Liu Zhanen and Others Are Vice Presidents

｜Dr. Craigh Gives a Lecture on the Benefits of Educational Groups｜

The first general meeting of the Shanghai International Education Society was held last night at the Chinese YMCA on Mintini Yin Road. Those in attendance included Dr. Liu Zhanen of Shanghai University, Kangpu, Acting Director of the Education Department of the Shanghai Municipal Council, Niu Sheng, Principal of Yinghua Bookstore, Father Moya of Jiangsaga College, Pan Fu, Acting Principal of the Church Girls' School, Chen Heqin, Director of the Chinese Education Department of the Shanghai Municipal Council, Dr. Ai La of St. John's University, Fu Ya, Principal of the Chinese School for the Blind, and more than 70 male and female teachers from famous schools in Shanghai. Dr. Wei Ke of the Chinese YMCA presided over the meeting. First, the chairman reported on the preparation of the society and elected Kangpu as president, and Dr. Wei Ke, Dr. Liu Zhanen, and Dr. Hols as vice presidents. Dr. Lin Falde, Bai Tuo Lai, Chen Heqin, Shi Shou Deng, Bai Er, Dr. Weiss Locke, Dr. Man Yin, and Ms. Yang were elected as members of the committee. After the election, Dr. Craigh, Doctor of Science from the University of London, gave a lecture on (the benefits of educational groups). He briefly stated that the establishment of the society can enable the education community in Shanghai to connect with each other, exchange knowledge, and maintain the power of the National Teachers' Association of the United Kingdom, as well as the history of industrial education in the United Kingdom. The technical schools in the United Kingdom were produced by mechanical vocational schools after several reforms. Government subsidies were initially based on passing certain examinations and the number of students. Teachers' salaries were also determined by the results of the examinations. After the government introduced the wine tax for the army and navy, it also allocated funds for education. The doctor detailed the entire method by which the local government education committee and the higher education committee handle education. Finally, he briefly spoke about the recent situation of various industrial schools in London. After the lecture, the doctor also answered questions from the guests regarding the process of teaching woodworking at Zhongshan Elementary School and the method of guiding textile technology in certain schools in the industrial area. Finally, Mr. Kangpu thanked Dr. Craigh on behalf of the guests. Mr. Shi Shou Deng of Gezhi Public School is the treasurer of the society and keeps the list of members. He collected membership fees before the meeting adjourned. More than 50 people joined the society that night, including eight international members.

French Concession Private Schools Discuss Subsidies 118

▲ More Than 30 Schools Respond

▲ Meeting This Afternoon at 1:00 PM to Discuss Methods

The French Concession in this city has a large area and a large population. However, there are only more than 40 primary and secondary schools in the concession. Among them, the only municipal school is the Bide No. 1 Elementary School, and the rest are private. Due to limited funding, they have not been able to expand as much as possible, causing many school-age children in the concession to suffer from a lack of opportunities to attend school. The neighboring Public Concession, since the Shanghai Municipal Council allocated subsidies, has received as much as 10,000 taels per year for many schools, and at least 1,000 taels per year. The development prospects of each school are limitless. If the French Municipal Council does not have a similar plan, and the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education is unable to establish more schools in the French Concession, then future private schools will inevitably seek school sites in the Public Concession, and the development of education in the French Concession will have even less hope. Ma Jiazhen, the Principal of Huadong Middle School, has recognized this and specifically advocated the proposal to request subsidies from the French Municipal Council. The local educational administrative authorities and the city party headquarters and the city education association have expressed great sympathy and will give it strong support. As for the private schools, more than 30 schools have responded, and it has been decided that a meeting will be held at 1:00 PM this afternoon at the Girls' Department of Huadong Middle School on Beile Road, Xujiahui Road to discuss methods.

The Municipal Bureau of Education Bans the Private Minben Elementary School 119

(Central News Agency) The private Minben Elementary School in Yu Kang Li, Chujia Bridge, French Concession, is the former private Huigong No. 3 Elementary School that was banned by the Jin Education Bureau. The content of the school was corrupt, and it falsely claimed to be registered with the Municipal Bureau of Education. After investigation, the bureau has sent a letter to the French Concession Police to close it down and confiscate the school equipment.

The Municipal Bureau of Education Plans to Inspect the Facilities of Civil Supplementary Schools 120

The Municipal Bureau of Education has established 48 civil supplementary schools in various districts this year, with a total of 54 classes, as reported in previous newspapers. The average number of students in each central civil supplementary school is over 100. The number of students in each mobile civil school and attached civil supplementary school is stipulated to be 40 per class, but most exceed the stipulation, and some particularly developed ones have reached over 80. In total, there are over 1,600 students in all civil schools and over 600 students in supplementary schools. The schools have now been open for more than a month. The Bureau of Education has stipulated that in addition to the inspectors from the Supervision Department distributing inspections, the principals of the central civil supplementary schools will conduct inspections by district, and the chiefs of the responsible departments and the directors of the civil supplementary education section will conduct inspections in turn to promote progress. Once the revised inspection form is printed, they will set off.

Faculty of Political Science and Law Raises Funds to Aid the Righteous Army 121

Students from the Shanghai Faculty of Political Science and Law on Jinshenfu Road, in view of the fact that the Northeast Righteous Army is fighting against the enemy in the cold in Eastern Province and lacks supplies and equipment, have launched a fundraising campaign to aid the Righteous Army. In addition to raising funds from all teachers and students of the school, the school's Tongru Chonghai Qixue Alumni Association, Guangming Society, Zhejiang Alumni Association, and Liangguang Alumni Association have organized a variety show and contacted ball games as a method of fundraising for the outside world.

Chizhi Wins A Group Championship in Disaster Relief Basketball Tournament 130

Yesterday They Defeated Tongji 40-27

John Jiangnan Wins the Right to the B Group Finals

Tonight's Women's and B Group Finals

B Group Finals Start at 6:00 PM

Women's Finals at 7:00 PM

The Chizhi and Tongji basketball teams competed for the A Group championship in the disaster relief basketball tournament last night at the Chinese Basketball Hall. As a result, Chizhi relied on their magical shooting and solid lineup to defeat Tongji 40-27 and win the championship. The two teams performed well, and the 300 to 400 spectators were all satisfied. The details are recorded below:

Tongji Takes the Lead First

The Tongji University team's rewards are not weak. In the preliminary round, they defeated John. Their ball skills were praised by the audience. When they competed with Chizhi, they took the lead first. The momentum was great, and they took the lead with 11 to 4. The audience was worried about Chizhi.

Chizhi Temporarily Gives In

At this point, Chizhi worked hard to dominate and strive to take the lead. Qian Dingshen and Yang Linyu tried wonderful shots many times. The score gradually got closer. Over time, they once surpassed the top with 14 to 13, one point ahead of Tongji. But with time running out, Tongji regained the upper hand and won the first half with 16 to 14. Chizhi temporarily gave in.

The Fierce Battle in the Second Half

Starting in the second half, Chizhi Qi’s forwards stood out and used wonderful tactics to form a team from front to back, and they got wonderful shots from Yang, Guo, and Qian. The points increased sharply. Although Tongji was unwilling to show weakness and worked hard to attack the door, they were helpless because the opponent was well-prepared and impenetrable. Perseverance and re-efforts were ultimately ineffective. As a result, Chizhi won with 40 to 27 and won the championship. Although Tongji lost, their performance was also exhausted, and it was not a crime of war.

China Youth Basketball League 135

Starts on the 15th of This Month

The China Youth Basketball League Association held its first committee meeting yesterday, chaired by Chairman Le Xiurong. At that time, the following matters were resolved: (1) The business and academic groups will each be divided into three divisions, namely Business 1, Business 2, Business 3, Academic 1, Academic 2, and Academic 3. (2) The competition will begin on November 15th, with competition times from 5:30 PM to 9:30 PM every Tuesday, Thursday, and Saturday. (3) New rules will be adopted, and the game time will be set at twenty minutes per half, with a lemon time of ten minutes. (4) If any team has outstanding procedures, they must be completed before November 12th, otherwise they will not be allowed to participate in the competition. (5) Applications received after October 31st will not be accepted. (6) If a participating team does not arrive at the venue within five minutes of the scheduled start time, it will be considered a forfeit. The clock time will be based on the clock in the China Youth Gymnasium.

Local News

The People's Food Association Plans to Establish Rural Public Warehouses 142

The Treasure Implementation Method Has Been Approved at the First Meeting

The Third Meeting Is Scheduled to Be Held in Suzhou on the 19th

This year's timing is appropriate, and the rice harvest is abundant. However, society is affected by the war, various industries are in decline, and the economy is depleted, leading to a disparity in the supply and demand of grain and a tragic drop in market prices. The impact on the livelihoods of farmers and the national economy is extremely significant. The Shanghai Local Association, therefore, invited the chambers of commerce of Nanjing and major rice-producing areas in Jiangsu Province to meet twice in Wuxi and Zhenjiang. Starting on the 28th of last month, the Jiangsu-Shanghai People's Food Regulation Association was established. The association held its second meeting in Shanghai the day before yesterday, and the implementation methods for establishing rural public warehouses were discussed. The details are recorded below:

Second Meeting: Jiangsu-Shanghai People's Food Regulation

The Association held its second committee meeting at the Shanghai Local Association at 7 PM on the 3rd of this month. The attendees included representatives from the Jiangsu Provincial Federation of Chambers of Commerce, the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, the Zhenjiang, Wuxi, and Wuxian Chambers of Commerce, including Hu Jianchun and Wang Xiaolai, and representatives from the Shanghai Local Association, including Shi Liangcai and Huang Renzhi, and others, more than ten people in total. He Yushu, Director of the Jiangsu Industrial Department, also personally attended the meeting in Shanghai. The meeting was chaired by Qian Sunqing, a representative from the Wuxi Chamber of Commerce. First, Yu Xiaochuan, a representative from the Zhenjiang Chamber of Commerce, Qian Sunqing, a representative from the Wuxi Chamber of Commerce, and Huang Renzhi, a representative from the Shanghai Local Association, reported on the progress of various matters and the situation of contact with various parties. Then, the draft implementation plan for establishing rural public warehouses in various places was discussed. After revising the wording, it was unanimously approved. Regarding the methods for contacting the financial sector, it was decided that the representatives attending the meeting should participate in the Shanghai Local Association's banking industry meeting tomorrow (i.e., yesterday) to discuss everything. It was also decided to recommend a representative to meet with Minister Song to petition. The petition was drafted by Huang Renzhi. Furthermore, it was resolved that the next meeting would be held in Suzhou on the 19th of this month.

Implementation Methods: The following are the implementation methods for establishing rural public warehouses in various places, officially issued by the Jiangsu-Shanghai People's Food Regulation Association: The market price of new grain has plummeted, and the farmers' hard work throughout the year cannot be sold promptly, and even if it is sold, it is not enough to repay debts and meet all living needs. This has a minor impact on the future livelihoods of farmers and a major impact on undermining the national economic foundation. According to reports from various parties, the situation is extremely urgent. The colleagues gathered twice in Wuxi and Zhenjiang to organize this association, seeking the circulation of grain and wheat in various provinces, the reduction and exemption of donations and taxes, the implementation of taxes on imported foreign rice, and the revitalization of the commercial and economic circulation. In particular, the establishment of rural public warehouses in rice-producing areas to receive rice and grain mortgages from farmers is considered the most effective direct relief method. Therefore, the implementation procedures have been carefully discussed, and the following methods are proposed for the reference and implementation of gentlemen who are enthusiastic about relief in rice-producing areas. Article 1: In all rice-producing areas, the original public organizations or specially formed groups should handle the establishment of rural public warehouses. Article 2: The above-mentioned organizations should simultaneously plan on-site and recommend local figures with outstanding reputations who are trusted by the financial community to be responsible for contacting local or nearby metropolitan financial institutions. Article 3: Local farmers' banks should take responsibility and be the initiators of this matter. Those who have not handled mortgages should promptly prepare to handle them. Those who have already handled them should find ways to expand them. If their strength is insufficient, they can join the local persons publicly recommended in the previous article to be responsible for contact and jointly proceed. Article 4: These public warehouses should be located in the center of the countryside to facilitate the nearby farmers to send mortgages of agricultural products. The location should be decentralized and should not be concentrated in one place. Article 5: These public warehouses are intended to benefit poor farmers, so the number of agricultural households sending mortgages of agricultural products may be limited per household to ensure that a wider range of people benefit. Article 6: The houses required for these warehouses may be borrowed from public temples or other buildings, or rented from private houses. In general, the site should be high and dry and convenient for transportation. Article 7: These warehouses shall receive agricultural products subject to mortgages at 70% to 80% of the market price to ensure fairness. Article 8: These warehouses shall receive agricultural products subject to mortgages, and according to the current situation, the interest rate shall be one percent per month. The warehouse rent, insurance, and all other expenses shall be calculated separately and shall be kept to a minimum. Article 9: If there are two or more financial institutions in a place that handle these warehouses, it is advisable to organize a joint office to handle them jointly. Article 10: If various places are preparing these warehouses and have determined the organization and recommended responsible personnel, and want to request a loan from a financial institution in a certain place, the organizations of this association in that place should jointly contact and assist in the process.

Wang Zhixin Talks: At noon yesterday, the association also held a meeting at the Shanghai Local Association to discuss methods for contacting the Shanghai financial community. After the meeting, according to Tu Zhixin, Director of the Jiangsu Provincial Farmers' Bank, speaking to the Central News Agency reporter, today's (i.e., yesterday's) afternoon meeting did not result in any concrete decisions. The difficulty lies in the issue of security guarantees for financial investors after the investment. This relief project is inherently the business that the Jiangsu Provincial Farmers' Bank should handle. However, because this relief must cover the entire province, the scope is large and the funds required are large. The Farmers' Bank is forced to ask various financial institutions to provide assistance. In places where farmers' branch offices have already been established and where storage warehouses have been set up, it is easy to implement. Those who have local wealthy merchants who can be trusted can also be asked to act as agents. Since the financial industry is not solely for the purpose of making profits, the Farmers' Bank is also willing to guarantee all parties, but these branch offices and warehouses are concentrated in the Jiangnan area and have not been able to cover the entire territory, and the total capacity of all the warehouses is only 100,000 to 120,000 dan. Therefore, although the various financial institutions are generally providing assistance now, how will the Farmers' Bank accept it to ensure that all farmers in the province enjoy its benefits and provide investors with the most reliable guarantees? This is the so-called difficulty. After several contacts, a part of the banks has added their consent, but I hope that the above-mentioned difficulties can be resolved as soon as possible, and that the various financial institutions can also cooperate and assist, so that the farmers will benefit a lot. The next meeting is scheduled to be held in Suzhou, but I am afraid I will not be able to attend. It has been decided to proceed first in places where farmers' banks and warehouses have already been established, he said.

Letter to the French Consul General

The French Concession Taxpayer Chinese Association sent a letter to the French Consul General, stating: "Respectfully, this is based on a letter from the French Concession Commercial Federation, stating that the various businesses on this road and the residents of Chengzhi Lane, Bulin Lane, Ji'an Lane, Yuqing Lane, Gaodi Lane, Hezhong Lane, and Taiyuan Fang have stated that the market is sluggish, rents are expensive, and it is difficult to bear. We request to promote rent reduction in order to maintain the market. Based on this, since the Shanghai 1.28 Incident, the market depression in the two concessions has been roughly the same. However, the Public Concession, bordering North Shanghai, has suffered more direct losses than the French Concession. However, before long, it was able to restore its former appearance, and considering the recent desolate scene of the French Concession, it has become increasingly obvious. In the past year, although the houses in the remote areas, once renovated, were rented out early before the completion of the work. Now, the city houses in the central area of Zhengjia Wood Bridge Street Hongyu Fang, etc., have been completed for a long time, and only a few have been rented out. These current situations are still obvious. As for the commercial situation, it is even more difficult. Although the appearance of the various businesses has to be exaggerated, most of them are strong on the outside but weak on the inside,勉爲支持, If this continues, it is inevitable that the situation will plummet, and in the near future, the French Concession, which has been gradually prospering for decades, will gradually degenerate and cannot be remedied. Therefore, we are especially reporting the situation and requesting your association to truthfully submit it to the French Consul General for review and give relief in order to maintain the market and conform to public opinion. Based on this, the various sections stated by the association are indeed facts. Our association believes that at present, in order to correct deviations and make up for shortcomings, it is not enough to reduce rents in order to maintain the market and stabilize people's hearts. However, if you want to reduce rents, it is useless if you do not first stabilize the land price. Because if the land price is first stabilized, the house price will also be stable. There is a close relationship between them. However, the current French Municipal Council has raised the land price in order to increase tax revenue, which is contrary to the market situation and is not appropriate. Your Consul General is coming to comfort us, and he will be able to understand the situation. You should make a decisive decision and quickly reduce the arbitrarily raised land price estimated by the current French Municipal Council, and allow our association to elect two Chinese members to participate in the Land Price Committee. We will be grateful. This is to the French Consul General, Merley, the French Concession Taxpayer Chinese Association.

After the Swiss Consul General in Shanghai is Promoted to Chargé d'Affaires, Sino-Swiss Relations Should Be Further Enhanced 146

The Chargé d'Affaires Office Will Be Located in Shanghai

Central News Agency reported: "Yesterday, Chinese and Western newspapers published news that the Swiss Federal Administrative Committee will promote the Swiss Consul General in Shanghai to Chargé d'Affaires in China. Yesterday morning, the Central News Agency reporter specifically visited Lao Di, the Swiss Consul General in Shanghai, at his consulate to inquire whether the office had received formal orders. As Lao Di was out on official business, the reporter was received by Tan Li Ke, the acting consul. The interview is recorded as follows:

Haven't Received Clear Orders Yet: According to Tan, he and others only saw in the newspapers the news that Lao Di, the Consul General in Shanghai, was promoted to Chargé d'Affaires in China. However, Sino-Swiss relations are becoming increasingly close, and the news is probably not a rumor. Therefore, the consulate firmly believes that a clear order will arrive in Shanghai soon. As for whether Lao Di will still serve concurrently as Consul General in Shanghai after the Consul General is promoted to Chargé d'Affaires, it is not yet known. However, it is dared to believe that the Chargé d'Affaires office will be located in Shanghai. As for the organization of the Chargé d'Affaires office, it will also wait until a clear order is received before requesting instructions.

Recent Situation of Swiss Nationals in China: Tan also said that according to the latest survey, there are a total of 480 Swiss nationals in China, of which 225 are in Shanghai. Swiss nationals who come to China are initially engaged in the silk industry, because the Swiss nationals who come to China are all from the city of Schaffhausen, Switzerland. The city is an industrial area, and the silk industry is one of Switzerland's famous products. However, after the Swiss nationals arrive in China, some have changed industries one after another. As for Chinese people traveling to Switzerland, the number is very large, mostly students. The Swiss government is quite preferential to Chinese citizens entering the country, and passport fees are not charged. Now that the Consul General in Shanghai has been promoted to Chargé d'Affaires, Sino-Swiss relations should be further enhanced in the future.

Proportion of Sino-Swiss Trade: Swiss goods exported to China in Sino-Swiss trade mainly include machinery, watches, silk, pigments, condensed milk sugar, etc. Chinese goods exported to Switzerland include raw silk, straw hat braids, tea monosodium glutamate, soy sauce, sausages, etc. According to a survey in 1930, Chinese exports to Switzerland totaled more than 10 million Swiss francs, and Swiss goods exported to China totaled 29 million Swiss francs. According to a survey in 1931, Chinese goods exported to Switzerland totaled more than 10 million Swiss francs, and Swiss goods exported to China totaled more than 19 million Swiss francs. The exact trade figures for this year are higher than last year. Tan continued to say that the Sino-Swiss trade treaty was signed in Tokyo as early as June 12, 1918.

Shanghai National Products Company Opens Today 147

Collecting Excellent Products from All Over the Country

The Shanghai National Products Company, located opposite the Hongmiao Temple on Nanjing Road, opens today. It is reported that the company's organization

at the beginning, was initiated by Wu Zhihao, Wang Xiaolai, Chen Depei, Fu Fangting, Lu Qisheng, and others, and the shares have been fully collected. More than 1,400 manufacturers are selling, with colorful and perfect products. Visiting the stores, there are silk, leather goods, woolen fabrics, Suzhou embroidery, lace, jewelry, clothing, and cosmetics departments, with novel patterns. Visiting the third floor, there are offices, wholesale departments, patriotic national products coupon offices, and foreign trade spot purchase departments. Observing the prices set for various goods, they are very low, and visitors from all walks of life are welcome. Shanghai National Products Co., Ltd.

Opening Declaration: Time has come to this day, the economic competition is increasingly fierce. It is appropriate that our country is a weak country with underdeveloped industries and a backward economy, forming a semi-colonial land. Now, the whole country, from the top to the bottom, is panic-stricken and engaged in promoting national products and saving the country through industry in order to revive the economy. However, after years of practice, little success has been achieved. The reason for this is certainly not one-sided. However, merely having concrete Shanghai National Products Company building drawings

advocacy without actual measures, and merely having individual production and sales without overall statistics, are the key to the conclusion. China has a vast territory and a large population. Raw materials and commodities vary from place to place. Or, what is produced in this place is what is needed in that country, or that country has an oversupply while this place has an over-demand. If we can adjust it accordingly, then production and sales will be commensurate, and supply and demand will correspond. Industry will naturally be easy to develop. Now, transportation in various places is inconvenient, and national products trading has no suitable location, so that producers wait to sell but cannot, and consumers want to buy but cannot. Therefore, how can we expect the development of industry and improve foreign trade? If we reverse this and guide it according to the situation and promote it according to the time, then our country's raw materials are superior to the world, enough to supply emerging industries with a surplus, and the customs are simple and honest, the labor is diligent and the salary is low, and the cost of commodities must be lower than that of Europe and the United States. It is easy to promote and sell well. Even in terms of existing industries, many are exquisite and unparalleled, with ingenious craftsmanship, such as the silks and satins of Jiangsu and Zhejiang, which are brilliant and pleasing to the eye, the porcelain of Jiangxi, which is smooth and clear, the embroidery of Suzhou and Hunan, which is realistic and vivid, the bamboo ware of Fenghua, which is ingenious and natural, and the carvings of Ningbo, which are lifelike. In addition, there are lacquerware in Fujian and summer cloth in Hubei, which are too many to enumerate. In terms of products, the leather goods of Beijing and Shaanxi are light, warm, and comfortable, especially in the mouth. In short, each province in our country has special products due to different climates and customs. If we can collect and promote them, it will also add luster to national products. The same

Page 14

People and others, in view of this, dare not overestimate themselves and organize Shanghai National Products Co., Ltd. in Shanghai, the economic center of the country, with the aim of collecting local products and industrial products from various provinces to form a national products trade center to meet the needs of supply and demand. Therefore, in addition to setting up retail stores, we also set up management, wholesale, promotion, consignment sales, and foreign trade departments to promote actively with a fearless spirit, so that our national products are complete in every beauty and reach far and wide, seeking to achieve the goal of saving the country through industry. No Turnaround in European and American Silk Sales

The silk industry has been in recession for years and has reached its peak. Out of the city's 106 single-reeling silk factories, many have closed down one after another. A reporter from the Xinsheng News Agency met with Shen Huachen, chairman of the Silk Manufacturers Association, yesterday. Jiangwan City Committee Reports to the Municipal Government on the Petition of Villagers 158

More than 3,000 women and children in the Jiangwan district petitioned the municipal commissioners of the district yesterday morning to restore civilian residences. The municipal commissioners of the district, together with representatives of various organizations in the district, reported the progress to the municipal government yesterday and asked for instructions. The Secretary-General of the Municipal Government, Yu Hongjun, received them and promised to find a way to provide relief. The details are recorded below.

Reporting the Progress Those who went to the Municipal Government to report yesterday included Wu Xuen, municipal commissioner of the district, Gu Shanzhang, member of the 7th District Party Department, Lu Yubin, executive of the Education Association, Zhong Yibo, director of the branch office of the Chamber of Commerce, and Wang Wujun, executive of the Farmers' Association. Secretary-General Yu received them. Wu Xuen, a member of the Jiangwan City Committee, reported on the progress. He said that the purpose of the petition was to request the construction of houses on the spot. One reason is that the civilian materials built by the local maintenance committee are not suitable for the lives of farmers. The second reason is that building houses in Dachang Miaohang in neighboring districts is more common, which makes them feel inferior. According to the recent survey, there are 301 households with 2,139 rooms damaged in the town, and 2,362 households with a total of 7,498 rooms damaged in the countryside. Currently, the reliable relief funds are 60,000 yuan from the local maintenance committee. After spending 39,000 yuan to build the First Civilian Memorial Village, there is still 21,000 yuan left, which is prepared for the construction of the Second Civilian Village. Now, the committee has slightly agreed to change the method to distribute it for scattered construction. The War Zone Rehabilitation Committee should allocate 25,000 yuan to Jiangwan for house construction, which has also been decided to be changed to relief. The total is 46,000 yuan. Assuming that each household needs to build one room, 2,362 rooms need to be built. If the cost per room is 100 yuan, it will cost 236,200 yuan, which is still short of 190,000 yuan. If the second poorest is not counted, deducting two-thirds, and removing the 46,000 yuan, there is still a shortage of 120,000 yuan. The Municipal Government should promptly allocate this fund to provide relief and benefit the people's livelihood.

Mr. Yu's Reply Secretary-General Yu replied that the disaster area in Jiangwan is significant, and the countryside is more severe than any other area. The housing problem in winter is extremely important. The Municipal Government has ordered the Municipal Social Bureau to allocate all of the existing relief fund of 25,000 yuan to Jiangwan to work with the municipal commissioners to properly plan relief methods. On the one hand, there are 21,000 yuan from the local maintenance committee, totaling 46,000 yuan, which is the first relief fund issued a month ago. On the other hand, the Rehabilitation Committee will be requested to raise funds for relief again, and the Ministry of Finance of the National Government will be requested to allocate funds for relief. In short, the government will do its best to provide assistance. He hopes that the gentlemen will tell the villagers not to misunderstand and to be careful not to overstep the boundaries.

Red Swastika Society Reports on the Binjiang Disaster 166

The Shanghai General Office of the China Southeast Main Branch of the World Red Swastika Society sent a letter to the Shanghai Charity Organizations Joint Relief Association for Northeastern Refugees yesterday, respectfully stating that they received a letter from the Binjiang Branch stating that since August 7th, the Songhua and Nenjiang rivers in this port have been overflowing and flooding, causing the dikes to break. The prosperous city has suddenly become a swamp. The disaster is extremely severe and unprecedented in more than a hundred years. Thanks to the repeated relief efforts of various charitable groups, many lives have been saved. However, the disaster is severe and the period is long, so long-term planning is still needed. In addition to the existing porridge factories, the number of disaster victims should be reviewed and porridge factories should be added appropriately to avoid freezing and starvation. The association has prepared more than 4,000 sets of relief clothing. The Changchun Branch has already placed 5,000 sets of relief clothing. In addition, there are still 10,000 sets of relief clothing, totaling about 20,000 sets. Compared with the number of people, the difference is huge, and preparations should continue. The survey of the disaster area, until the end of September, roughly covered the upstream and downstream areas along the Songhua River, from Xiaojiangzi on the north bank of the Songhua River to the mouth of the Hulan River, about 120 miles east and west, and 40 miles north and south, totaling 193 villages, with approximately 3,200 households awaiting relief, totaling approximately 22,400 refugee women and children. In Jiangnan Fuyiadian, from 13th Street eastward to Taipingqiao Sankeshu Huangsanzuzi and other places, there are approximately 4,500 households, with approximately 27,400 refugees, women, and children awaiting relief, totaling 50,000 people. The shelters and porridge factories set up serve more than 7,000 people daily, requiring 50 train cars of millet per month, each car containing 30,000 catties, costing 800 yuan per car, totaling 40,000 yuan. It is estimated that 240,000 yuan will be needed for six months. The problem of emergency relief cannot be delayed in the slightest. The weather is getting colder rapidly, and the outside of the Great Wall is extremely cold. If the disaster victims do not die from the floods, they may die from hunger and cold. The association has tried its best to raise funds, but it is difficult to achieve universal coverage. Moreover, the counties bordering Jiang Province have also suffered from floods, and they should be rescued together regardless of boundaries. We hope to publicize widely and earnestly request various charitable groups to jointly provide relief, which will be of immeasurable merit. Accordingly, a copy of the letter is sent for your information and instructions.

Appeal for Bandit Disasters in Taihu and Susong, Anhui Province 167

The Shanghai Temporary Righteous Relief Association for Disaster Areas in Henan, Anhui, and Hubei received a fast mail from the Anhui Taihu Post-Disaster Committee yesterday, stating that Taihu is connected to Yinghuo in the north and Xinshihuang in the west. Since the Red Bandits invaded last autumn, more than a thousand people have been killed and kidnapped in Baiyang Zhenjun Yuyu Wang Qiaxi Qiantan Qingtian Nanzhuang Yangsheng and other places. Clothing and food have been looted, the old and weak have been abandoned in ditches, and the young and strong have fled in all directions. The suffering has lasted for nearly a year. This time, the bandits from Jinjiazhai fled into the county, passing through the fourth, second, and third districts before fleeing to Susong and then to Huangjiaihe in the first district and Siqianhe in the fifth district. Thanks to Tang's blockage, they fled back to the second, third, and fourth districts from Susong. In total, each time the number of people was more than 10,000, occupying the area for about half a month. In addition, hundreds of miscellaneous groups have never had a peaceful day. Wherever they go, food and clothing are exhausted, and even utensils are destroyed and people are killed by fire. The remaining survivors have suffered another disaster. We beg your association to send personnel to provide relief, and also telegraph the Central Relief Committee and charitable groups in Beijing and Shanghai to provide relief. We are eagerly awaiting your command.

Also, a joint letter from the Susong County Party Department, Finance Bureau, Chamber of Commerce, Education Association, and District Offices stated that on October 7th, the remaining fierce bandits from Jinjiazhai suddenly invaded Susong from Xinshichun Zhangjiaxin in the northwest, which is connected to Hubei, Xinshichun, Huangmei, and Taihu. They entered the Changhe Kabei Bath area in the western part of the county. After the hunters did their best to resist, the bandit forces were too large and the strength of the county was too weak. On the evening of the 8th, they went straight to the Hankou and took Aikou Village via Bijiating. Our security team resisted for four hours, but due to insufficient strength, they retreated to the Erbu Temple and the county seat. The bandits went straight from Aikou to Hualiangting in Fengchezhuang and other places, fleeing into the Xiyuan Mountains. The people's houses, belongings, clothing, and food in the villages they passed were all looted. The 47th Division of the National Salvation Army, led by Li Guo, followed them into the Xiyuan Mountains. The bandits fled from the mountain roads into Zhifeng Henanchong Guyuan and other places in the Beixiang Yuanlin Village, robbing houses, setting fires, killing people, and committing robberies, which was even worse than when they entered the country. Fortunately, Tang Brigade Chen and Yang Yuan rushed to the rescue overnight and fought with the bandits. However, in the area where the bandits passed, the residences and people were left empty. Although they have tried every means to gather and seek a livelihood, the residences, livestock, clothing, and furniture are all gone. Winter is approaching, how will they survive? Moreover, the autumn harvest grain has been robbed and eaten. In this situation, they will inevitably die of starvation. We earnestly request your association to consider the hundreds of thousands of disaster victims who have suffered this catastrophe and have no means of living, and quickly provide emergency relief to save the refugees. We will be grateful beyond measure.

Sichuan National Salvation Association Representatives Arrive in Shanghai 168

Inspect Factories and Investigate Domestic Goods

The Shanghai Sichuan Merchants Association sent a letter to the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce yesterday, stating that according to a letter from the Sichuan People's National Salvation Congress, Sichuan is located in a remote western region and has important relationships with Yunnan, Guizhou, and Shaanxi provinces. It has now been discovered that many French counterfeit goods are shipped from Shanghai, all of which are repackaged and counterfeit. Therefore, Standing Committee members Li Kaixian and Dong Jiaji were specially appointed as representatives of the association to come to Shanghai to conduct a thorough investigation of various factories and the true state of domestic goods, and to be responsible for contacting local patriotic organizations to discuss progress. The two representatives, Li and Dong, have arrived in Shanghai and are in contact with the Chamber of Commerce for all matters.

Shanghai Social Bureau Mediates Taikoo Labor Dispute Yesterday 169

Wait for the Compradors to Meet and Determine Standards

Sign the Mediation Agreement Next Thursday

After the British Taikoo Company laid off middle-class workers on various Yangtze River routes, a labor dispute occurred, and the situation was very serious. The Central Committee and the Ministry of Industry ordered the municipal government to handle it properly. Although the government has mediated repeatedly, it has not been resolved. Yesterday afternoon at 2:00 pm, the Social Bureau held another mediation session.

Mediation Process: Representatives Zhu Huanqing and Zhu Ruiqing of the China Shipping Mutual Aid Association, and Lu Rongzhi and Zhou Xiaoting of the Seafarers' Middle Class Guild attended. Representatives of middle-class workers from Taikoo and Jardine, China Merchants, and Datong attended as observers. Dai Youheng of the Municipal Party Committee was present. Zhu Guilin, a mediator from the Social Bureau, presided over the meeting, and Wang Zhiqin recorded the minutes. First, the chairman briefly stated that this case has been mediated repeatedly, but no progress has been made. Today's mediation hopes that everyone will make concessions in order to resolve the issue and avoid expansion. Then, the business director stated that although he has repeatedly requested the company, the company insists on not agreeing to the first item in accordance with the China Merchants Bureau's method, believing that if it cannot be implemented now, the five items proposed will be postponed. However, the business director hopes to devise a good plan to achieve a permanent solution. The labor representative stated that although the company is willing to postpone implementation, the workers hope to find a comprehensive and fundamental solution to avoid future disputes. The chairman and the party committee representative then strongly persuaded each side.

Principles Passed: The principles for resolution are determined as follows: 1. In the future, the Taikoo Company's middle-class workers on the Yangtze River routes will only fill vacancies and not be supplemented, in order to rectify the situation (the standards will be determined by the business director). 2. The business director will formulate service rules for middle-class workers, but they must be implemented after being approved by the主管官署. 3. If a dispute arises between the business director and the workers in the future, it should be submitted to the主管官署 for verification. Both parties agreed to the principles. However, the comprador representative requested that the consent of all the compradors be obtained and the standards for middle-class workers on each route be specified. Finally, the chairman announced the adjournment of the meeting. After the compradors pass the resolution at the meeting, another mediation signing meeting will be convened next Thursday.
