Qianzhuang Guarantor Counterfeits Seal to Obtain Funds 176

Sun Rongde Substitutes Plum for Peach

Pan Housheng Files Criminal Lawsuit

It is customary in the Shanghai Qianzhuang industry that if a Qianzhuang customer has a guarantor, the Qianzhuang should send the customer's name, account number, and passbook to the guarantor, who in turn delivers the passbook to the customer. If the customer wants to stop transacting with the Qianzhuang, he should also send the passbook to the original guarantor to return it to the Qianzhuang to complete the procedure. This kind of circulation procedure is intended to clarify the guarantor's responsibility and has been practiced for many years with few malpractices. Recently, Pan Housheng, owner of the Shengho Xiang Store on Gansu Road, because of his financial dealings with the Lianyi Qianzhuang on Sichuan Road, followed the Qianzhuang industry practice and requested Sun Rongde, a shareholder and manager of the Xiefengyong Woolen and Foreign Goods Store in Zhengjia Bridge, to be his guarantor. At the end of February last year, because he no longer wanted to continue the financial dealings, Pan sent the transaction passbook to Sun Rongde, asking him to return it to the Lianyi Qianzhuang to complete the procedure. Unexpectedly, Sun not only did not return the passbook, but also falsely carved a seal with the words "Shengho Xiang," impersonating him to continue transacting with Lianyi, and defaulting on a huge amount of money from Lianyi. At first, the Qianzhuang did not know that Sun Rongde was cheating, but later, when settling the accounts, they learned of this substitution trick. Pan Housheng believed that Sun should not have falsely carved the Shengho Xiang seal, which was tantamount to fraud, so he hired lawyer Zhu Sitifei and filed a criminal lawsuit against Sun in the First Special District Local Court, requesting his arrest and punishment for forgery under Article 234 of the Criminal Law. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Huang of the court opened a trial. After the plaintiff's lawyer Zhu Sifei explained the intention of the lawsuit, the court immediately questioned the two parties about the circumstances of the case and instructed them to go outside to conduct a reconciliation in order to settle the dispute. If a reconciliation cannot be reached, a date will be set for retrial.

He also said to his wife, Wang, to be fair, and that he had been harmed by Yang Delin, etc. Wang Yinshan confessed that he was 30 years old, from Huzhou. The Case of the Gang of Robbers with Numerous Crimes 178

Yesterday, the Court Rendered Separate Judgments

Detectives Lu Gengsheng and Yang Beisheng of the Yulin Road Police Station, previously arrested fourteen individuals, including robbers Li Yucai, Ren Si, and a woman named Wan Chenshi, at locations such as No. 806 Huaji Road, No. 104 Seymour Road, and Jinsheng Road. Investigations revealed that between June 14 of last year and October of this year, these individuals, armed and organized, committed robberies at residences and businesses including: He Deshen at No. 942 Yuanfang Road, Xia Jinshi at No. 74 Pingliang Road, Jiang Donglai at No. 5 Huade Road, Zhang Amao at No. 448 of the same road, Huang Zhiting at No. 578 Baikai'er Road, Gui Nanzhen at No. 5 Fenzhou Road, and Weng Tanzhuo Pawnshop at No. 1384 Dong Yangshupu Road. The stolen items included jewelry and silver coins valued at over 2,000 yuan. Along with the arrest, two pistols and thirteen bullets were seized. All were handed over to the First Special District Court. After interrogation and conclusion of the case, they awaited sentencing. Yesterday morning, Judge Wu Zhen of the Third Criminal Court sentenced Li Yucai and Ren Si to sixteen years of imprisonment each. Feng Er, Wang Desheng, Sun Xiaogongzi, were sentenced to fifteen years each. Sun Huarong was sentenced to twelve years, Wan Chenshi to nine years, and Yang Chunjiang and Gong Junqing to ten years each. Lu A'gen, Zhang Chongli, and Zhang Guangyuan were sentenced to six years each, Yang Weikai to five years, and Ju Zhangshi to one year. Before the judgment becomes final, the number of days of detention will be counted with two days equivalent to one day of imprisonment. The two pistols and twelve bullets were confiscated. After the sentencing, Attorney Tian Yinqi of the police station stated that Li Yucai, Ren Si, and eight others had committed numerous robberies in the French Concession. Detectives from the French Police Station were sent to the court to request their transfer. However, Ren Si is still facing a murder charge, and the police station will file a separate lawsuit. He requested a temporary detention. Detective Cui Zhenguo of the French Police Station submitted an official document stating that, with the exception of Ren Si, they requested the transfer of the remaining individuals. Judge Wu also ordered that Li Yucai, Yang Chunjiang, Feng Er, Sun Huarong, Sun Xiaogongzi, Wang Desheng, and the woman Wan Chenshi be handed over to Cui Zhenguo for transfer to the Second Special District Local Court of Jiangsu Shanghai. After the trial, they will be returned to this court for execution of the sentences.

Record of the Visit to the New Italian Postal Ship "Conte Verde" 184

It Takes Only Twenty-Three Days from Shanghai to Italy

Since the Italian postal ship company has added express liners, it only takes 23 days from Shanghai to Europe, setting a new record for fast travel. Since the start of the service, the number of passengers has been increasing day by day. In addition to the original "Conte Rosso" and "Gange" vessels, the company has transferred the largest and fastest new postal ship "Conte Verde" from Italy to Shanghai to increase capacity in order to meet the demand. Yesterday, the company invited people from all walks of life in Shanghai to visit the new ship. Many Chinese and Westerners attended. The ship also provided refreshments. The situation is recorded as follows:

Beautiful Ship Body The "Conte Verde" is a newly built express postal ship with a tonnage of 19,000 tons, which is larger than the "Conte Rosso". The beauty of the layout of the first-class cabins, dining halls, halls, dance halls, writing rooms, smoking rooms, gyms, children's rooms, etc. on the ship is truly superior to that of a palace. The carpets are made of silk, and the utensils are specially made. Every table and chair is valuable. The first-class rooms are also equipped with bathrooms, which are spacious and comfortable. It is unprecedentedly excellent postal ship in Central Europe. Moreover, it has a very high speed and can travel 23 nautical miles per hour. It only takes 44 hours from Shanghai to Hong Kong and only 23 days to Italy. It can be called a sea palace on the Central European route.

Crowded with Guests The ship arrived in Shanghai one day and stopped at the Qichang Wharf in Pudong. Yesterday afternoon at 5:00 p.m., the company specially sent two small steamships to the Xinguang Wharf to welcome the guests who came to visit. There were one thousand several hundred Chinese and Westerners, including Huang Boqiao, Beide Post Office Manager Bilu, Chamber of Commerce Chairman Wang Xiaolai, Taikoo Dabang Paileis, Zheng Jun, representatives from the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, etc. Luso, the general manager of the Italian Post Office, Xie Li Gelanxi, and Chinese directors Shao Cai hosted the guests warmly on the ship and guided the visit. Italian Minister to China, Qi Yinuo, also came to the ship and mingled among the guests.

Treating the Guests The ship specially prepared tea, snacks, and Western food, and a dance floor and dining hall were opened on Deck B. Many Chinese and Western guests participated in the dance. Then, they had dinner until 7:30 p.m. before sending the guests back to Shanghai. The ship is scheduled to depart on its maiden voyage to Italy on the 7th of this month. It is reported that Lieutenant General Kai Lai, Commander of the Far East Fleet of the British Navy, will take the ship to Europe. Mr. Zhang Fakui, the Fourth Army Commander of China, will take the ship from Hong Kong to Italy, and then transfer to Germany and France.

Temporary Cancellation of the Yangtze River Import Lightship 191

Replaced by a Gas Buoy

Shipping Notice No. 1036 of the Maritime Department of the General Office of the Customs, states, "Regarding the announcement, I have received an order from the General Tax Commissioner to investigate the Yangtze River Import Lightship belonging to the Jianghai Customs, which is berthed at the import area of the Yangtze River waterway, and it is necessary to enter the dock for repairs. It should be temporarily cancelled and replaced by a gas buoy to facilitate navigation. It is scheduled to be implemented around November 22 of this year. The replacement buoy is 10 feet in diameter and is decorated with alternating red and black horizontal lines. An intermittent white light is placed on it, flashing once every eight seconds, that is, flashing for four seconds each. Once the lightship is repaired, it should still be driven back to its original location, and the replacement buoy should be removed. The relevant departments shall comply accordingly. It is hereby announced to all Chinese and foreign shipping merchants that they should be fully aware of this matter. Furthermore, it should be known that there will be no further announcement regarding the cancellation and return of the lightship. This is hereby announced. October 31, 21st year of the Republic of China, Karmer, Acting Inspector of the Maritime Department."

Letter to the Editor 207

To the Editor: In your newspaper's local news section on the 4th of this month, you published a report about the death of a patrolman from our factory. The facts stated in that report are, upon verification, largely inconsistent with the situation at the time. We hereby list the inaccuracies as follows: 1. The female worker Zhang Wangshi resisted inspection and grabbed the patrolman Ren Yuanshun's collar. She was persuaded to stop, and the patrolman did not slap her face. As for Fu Rusong and Ru Gaoge being detained, it was because the two of them, taking advantage of the crowd gathered at the factory gate, first broke into the gate and violently attacked Ren Yuanshun, leading to their detention. They were neither hung up nor pursued. 2. When the deceased, Chen Huahai, fell to the ground injured, his head was towards the factory wall and his feet towards the river. At that time, all those outside the factory gate were workers and nearby idlers. All patrolmen remained inside the gate. Since the deceased's head was facing inwards, it can be seen that the bullet came from outside. Furthermore, when patrolman Zhou Zhangmu saw Chen being shot down, he fired his gun in self-defense. The bullet hit the cement on the factory gate, and the traces are still there for verification. 3. The deceased, Chen Huahai, was not carrying a gun at the time. The gun was found later in his bedroom and taken away by the Sixth District police chief. 4. The population in the Tanzizhen area is very mixed, and they often create trouble with the factory. When this incident occurred, there were many idlers gathered in front of the factory gate. While the workers may be said to be unarmed, can it be guaranteed that those outside the factory were also unarmed? The above are the actual facts at the time. Your newspaper's account, we believe, was due to the reporter mistakenly adopting hearsay. Therefore, we specially send this letter to your chief editor, requesting that the above facts be published in the "Letter to the Editor" column to provide a correction and reveal the truth. Respectfully, to the Shen Bao newspaper, from Yong Yu Heji Textile Company, November 4th.

Special Document

Judge Feetham's Report on Conditions in the Shanghai International Settlement, Volume IV (13) 208

15. The aforementioned regulations are further supplemented by certain rules or budgetary ordinances, such as the following:

(The Council shall not vote on any expense unless the Finance Committee has considered it and submitted a report.)

In addition, there is another safeguard to prevent the Council from committing to increased expenditure based on suggestions that have not been financially considered. This is the regulation often stipulating that individual Councillors' suggestions (which would result in increased Council expenditure) should be subject to a procedure for submission to a committee for consideration (Note 6).

Taking the Health Committee as an example, according to the rules mentioned in the previous section, any suggestion regarding the adoption of public health measures must be submitted to the Health Committee for consideration. If the committee's report is in favor, then according to the rules cited in Section 14 above, the funds required for the expenditure due to the adoption of the Health Committee's suggestion must also be reported by the Finance Committee. Therefore, the Council has two layers of safeguards to prevent the acceptance of any suggestions involving expenditure whose results have not been thoroughly studied.

16. I therefore recommend that any plan for the development of the committee system should specifically consider how to define the functions of the Finance Committee of the Public Works Department through rules of procedure or other ordinances, and how to charge the committee with the same responsibilities as those stipulated in the regulations and rules I have cited (Note 7).

(Note 1) See Item 10 of the reform plan proposed in Chapter VI of Part 5 of this report.

(Note 2) This type of expenditure is classified as basic expenditure.

(Note 3) Regarding this argument, please refer to the following financial regulations. According to these regulations, under a more fully developed committee system, the relevant committee must submit recommendations to the Council before proceeding with matters prepared in the annual budget proposal.

(If the committee believes that the time has come to proceed with the matters prepared in the annual budget proposal or to implement the purchases prepared in the budget, the committee must first submit this recommendation for proceeding or purchasing to the Council, specifying the items mentioned in the budget proposal, and request the Council's approval.) (Johannesburg Municipal Financial Ordinance, Article 10)

(Note 4) I believe that it is unnecessary to quote the part of the statement specifically discussing this type of regulation, as that part specifies the details that should be listed in the register of items to be purchased (including the estimated prices) and includes various rules regarding soliciting quotations and inviting bids, as well as various provisions for ordering in emergencies.

(Note 5) See Appendix 42(A).

(Note 6) See Appendix 42(B)(3).

(Note 7) See Appendix 42(C) for a sample of the scope of authority of the Finance Committee.

Chapter III Appointment and Tasks of Auditors 209

1. The issue of auditing the Public Works Department's accounts has been previously discussed (Note 1) and pointed out (Note 2). Although the Land Regulations stipulate (Article 12) that (the accounts of the Board of Directors shall be audited) and that (the results of the audit) shall be announced at the annual meeting, there are no regulations regarding how the auditors should be selected, how they should be compensated, or what their position is in terms of tenure security. What has been noted as necessary (Note 3) is that regulations should be added regarding the appointment and qualifications of auditors, the nature of their tasks, and the security of their tenure, so that the independence of the auditors' position can be permanently guaranteed.

2. In the proposed reform plan C, two levels of recommendations were made regarding this issue: (1) Auditors should be elected by the annual meeting of taxpayers in the future. To avoid difficulties arising from the inability of the two taxpayers' meetings (foreign and Chinese) to agree on the same candidate, a provision may be established that if they cannot agree, the two taxpayers' meetings may elect their respective auditors. (2) The tasks of the auditors must also be defined, and the nature of the report that must be prepared when verifying the annual revenue and expenditure accounts must also be disclosed.

3. According to the provisions of the existing Land Regulations, the accounts of the Public Works Department (shall be audited). Although this provision seems to have been interpreted as meaning that the accounts of the Public Works Department should be independently audited by suitably qualified individuals who are neither employees of the Public Works Department nor directors of the Board of Directors, the meaning of this interpretation is not explicitly stated in the regulations. Therefore, it is necessary to clearly stipulate it, so as not to violate the practice that has been implemented and to ensure that the principle of independent auditing is permanently acknowledged.

4. The implementation of this principle is of particular importance in the International Settlement, because the system of having public authorities' accounts independently audited by legitimate individuals and publishing the results annually for public inspection is rarely recognized in China.

5. Any system for auditing public accounts that is sufficient, to a certain extent, to ensure sound and honest financial management must possess the following characteristics:

(1) The auditor should have the proper qualifications to perform the duties of an auditor. The auditor should be in an independent position with respect to the government office or agency whose accounts they are auditing.

(2) The auditor should have sufficient power to facilitate the auditing process. (3) The results of the audit should be published for public knowledge.

6. The maintenance of this system in the International Settlement, in addition to benefiting the handling of matters within the Settlement, is sufficient to demonstrate the value of this system for general public administration in practice (Note 5) and to promote the expansion of the scope of recognition of this value.

7. I will now discuss in detail the regulations that need to be added regarding the issue of auditing the Public Works Department's accounts, in order to supplement the recommendations that have already been made.

A. Qualifications of Auditors and Methods of Appointment

8. I now suggest that a regulation should be established to ensure that the personnel used to audit the accounts of the Public Works Department should be suitably qualified individuals who are neither directors nor employees of the Public Works Department. The term "suitably qualified individuals" should be interpreted as referring to individuals who, according to their national laws, are recognized as being able to perform the duties of accountants and auditors and who have been performing these duties in Shanghai for at least five years.

9. It has been suggested above that future auditors should be elected by the annual meeting of taxpayers, and that the election should be conducted by voting. If the plan to hold separate annual meetings for Chinese and foreign taxpayers is adopted, then each of these annual meetings will have the right to elect auditors. If the two annual meetings cannot agree on electing the same individual as auditor, then there may be two auditors. As far as I know, this method has been adopted in auditing the accounts of Shanghai companies, and apart from the additional expenditure involved, there is no serious objection in practical terms.

10. Regarding the election of auditors by the taxpayers' meeting, a rule must be established to ensure that the list of nominated auditor candidates is submitted to the Board of Directors several days before the meeting, so that there is sufficient time to review the qualifications of each candidate and notify the voters of the nominated candidates. I suggest that the list of nominated candidates should be submitted to the Board of Directors at least three weeks before the scheduled date of the election of auditors. This list should be signed by a prescribed number of taxpayers who are qualified to vote at the taxpayers' meeting. The task of reviewing this list is to determine whether the persons nominated are qualified. This review should be entrusted to a committee of the Board of Directors or an auditor appointed by the Board of Directors. (To be continued)

Free Talk

Random Notes

Reserving Seats 210

— Zhan Lu

The grand and lively 10th World Olympic Games have passed, and the 11th is scheduled to be held in Berlin in 1936. According to a Berlin telegram: It is said that although the next Olympic Games are far away, many member states have already reserved seats in Berlin with the World Sports Committee. Among them, students from a certain middle school in the United States have purchased 1,000 of the best seats. The news sparked a discussion between Mr. A and Mr. B:

Mr. A said: American students' concept of sports is almost like a second life. The year 1936 is still four years away, but they have seriously pre-purchased 1,000 excellent seats. How far-sighted are American students! How strong and enthusiastic is the American students' interest in the Olympics!

Mr. B said: Seeing others, I think of myself. China is also one of the member states of the 10th Olympic Games, but only Liu Changchun participated in the games, which shows the indifference of the Chinese to world sports! Even those who participate in the games are not so enthusiastic; even less do they pre-purchase seats.

Mr. X, who was listening nearby, came over and said a few witty words:

You shouldn't boost others' morale and diminish your own prestige! Who said that there are no Chinese students who pre-purchase seats for the Olympics? The three male students next door to my humble abode and the three female students next door have reserved good seats for the Olympics many times. Although they didn't pre-purchase 1,000 excellent seats, they always pre-purchase six seats each time, more than 20 times a month. Their interest in the Olympics is no less than that of American students!

Mr. A and Mr. B didn't know that he was speaking wittily, but they asked him in detail about the reason.

Don't doubt it, let me tell you the truth; the good seats reserved by the male and female students next door are not the seats for the Olympic Games, but the seats in the Paramount Theater during the summer; ha ha!

Mr. X said with a smile.

Chairman Lin 211

— Fu Hongmeng

—Two Things on the Way Back South—

According to general speculation, Chairman Lin's return south this time has something to do with the political situation in Fujian Province. In fact, Chairman Lin is just Chairman Lin, and the political situation in Fujian Province is just the political situation in Fujian Province. Everyone is not related. Yesterday, a friend came to Shanghai from Fujian and told the readers about the two greatest events in Chairman Lin's return to the south, so that they can be used as materials for writing celebrity anecdotes in the future.

1. Recommendation of Staff Members. Chairman Lin is, after all, a good gentleman. When he arrived in Fuzhou, he felt that after returning to his hometown for many years, it was not easy to comfort the villagers. After all, he was a little embarrassed, so he issued two handwritten notes, introducing Shao Junping as the inspector of the Public Security Bureau and Lin Dazhan as the deputy director of the Advertising Management Office of the Public Security Bureau. Unexpectedly, the Public Security Bureau was recently reorganized. It is said that the two members recommended by Chairman Lin are uneasy about their positions. It is a pity that the commemoration left by Chairman Lin's return to the south cannot last forever!

2. Clam Salted Beltfish. Although Chairman Lin has a high position and salary, he has never forgotten the taste of his hometown. This time he returned to the south, he brought a lot of local flavors of clams (hard shells like clams) and salted beltfish, so everyone competed to offer these two things to him. As a result, clams suddenly sold for ten copper coins per catty, and salted beltfish cost half a price per head. This is also the most memorable thing. It is said that these two things are the greatest in Chairman Lin's return to the south, so we also have a record of the price!

Mahjong Sutra 212

— Qiu Zhaowei

—One of the National Treasures—

Chinese people like to gamble, using gambling as a pastime, entertainment, and a means of making a living. Among these (gambling entertainments), mahjong is the most advanced, elegant, and widespread. Nowadays, young girls of thirteen or fourteen in urban middle-class families certainly understand (the Mahjong Sutra). If you walk into a tea house in a remote village, you will definitely hear the sound of mahjong. From scholars and officials to peddlers and porters, men and women, old and young, all walks of life, if you don't know mahjong, what a (wronged death)! (Bamboo battle) (Game of the square city), what elegant terms! I have nothing to call it, I call it (National Gambling) or (National Art), to join the ranks of (National Treasures), but my intention is not to promote it.

It is said that in a certain period, mahjong was appreciated by Westerners, so it was exported in batches, and many people became rich and famous by serving as mahjong instructors for Westerners. This is really a great and glorious thing.

Therefore, even if China perishes, China's art, mahjong, will be immortal forever!

Chinese people are the most leisurely, gentle, and particular about entertainment; and Chinese people are also the smartest and most able to (fight wits). Mahjong is really the most suitable thing. Chinese people are talented mahjong players. Hundreds of years ago, the Chinese created mahjong, passed it down from generation to generation, and have promoted it to the world, which is as great as queues, small feet, and opium smoking. Just imagine, four people are sitting around a square table, plus (spectators), concentrating, with uncertain hands and eyes, like crazy and obsessed all night long. Chinese entertainment is a symbol of the state of lung disease! The Chinese are a nation with lung disease through and through!

I tell you, in terms of (fighting wits), the Japanese are much stronger than our compatriots. Although we have many mahjong veterans, they may not lose when playing mahjong with the Japanese. They also have works such as (Advanced Tactics of Mahjong Game) (Secret of Chinese Mahjong Battle), but we don't, which should be a shame.

Talking About Cigarette Butts 213

— A Middle School Student

—Also a Kind of Skill—

No matter who it is, you must have a skill to make a living. If you don't have a special skill, then you will only starve to death. Even picking up cigarette butts requires a special skill. If you don't reach a high level, you may not even get two cents for picking up cigarette butts all day long. According to those who are experienced in picking up cigarette butts, they have been picking up cigarette butts for more than ten years. The number of cigarette butts they have picked up before and after is no less than hundreds of thousands. He goes to pick up cigarette butts in the area of ​​the Dongxin Bridge in the French Concession every afternoon after eating. On average, he can pick up one every two steps. But although the income is large, the quality is very poor. This is probably because the cigarette brands are mostly (Lianzhu brand) (Golden Mouse brand), etc.!

From south to Xiafei Road, from afternoon to midnight, it can be said that the pedestrians are endless. There are people of the upper, middle and lower classes. Therefore, the cigarette butts picked up can also be divided into three classes｜upper, middle and lower. Generally (compradors) (young masters) often discard them on the ground after smoking only half a cigarette. The butts are long and the quality of the cigarette is good. Most of them are (Carillac) (White Snow Pack), etc. This kind of cigarette butt can be regarded as the upper class. The general middle class mostly smoke (Beauty Brand) (Red Snow Pack), etc. The butts are neither long nor short. This kind of cigarette butt can be regarded as middle class. As for the lower class, they also want to stroll on the road and open their eyes. But the cigarettes they smoke have short butts and poor quality.

Nanjing Road is a gathering place for general foreign masters. Especially in the area of ​​the Rising Sun Building. The cigarettes smoked by foreign masters are of course foreign cigarettes｜at least one dollar a pack. And foreigners are very generous. They throw them away after taking a few puffs. If you are lucky, you can sell the cigarette butts you pick up every day for more than one dollar!

After nine o'clock, the general night owls began to move. Groups of (Shanghai young masters) (modern young ladies) (social stars) all walked into this soul-destroying place. Before they walk in, they must throw the cigarette butts outside first. You only need to guard a few hours, and you are guaranteed to return fully loaded. And they are all top-quality goods.

Random Notes on Planting 214

— Yun

—Fruit Trees Worth Introducing—

I am a follower of Tao Yuanming. Because the place where I live is only suitable for walking on the road of agriculture, I am engaged in agricultural affairs, but the result of the engagement is always failure. In the spring of the 14th year of the Republic of China, I bought a lot of fruit trees in Ningbo and started my agricultural work. The garden I planted was 20 acres, and the fruit trees I planted were 1,500 trees. When I first planted fruit trees, I estimated that I would definitely make a fortune after three years? Unexpectedly, in the third year, because the fruits were too small and the taste was not good, I could not exchange them for money. This was my first failure. Later, I bought 1,000 peach seedlings in Shanghai. In the third year, the result was the same as last time. I suffered these two major failures. The heart of returning to farming had long been cold.

In the spring of the year before last, I had a friend who bought dozens of kinds of fruit trees from Hefeng Agricultural and Forestry Farm in Pinghu. He took one tree of each kind and sent it to me for trial planting. After planting it, I felt that it was developing very well. This is only the second year, and the peaches have already borne very large and sweet fruits. My heart of returning to farming suddenly turned from cold to hot again. Therefore, I ordered 2,000 trees from Hefeng Agricultural and Forestry Farm in Pinghu, preparing to carry out my third planting work. I will also talk about these few sentences to introduce to comrades. (Pay respect)

Crossroads of Death (5) 215

— Fan Yanqiao

2. After Adapting to the Times

This series of orders exhausted Aigu again. Fortunately, she had a strong memory. She agreed, walked out, and tried to memorize the important and difficult to understand technical terms, chanting (lotus seed soup), (electric stove), (coal stove). When she arrived in the kitchen, she was fortunate enough not to disgrace her mission and told the newcomer one by one. However, she switched the (electric stove) and (coal stove). The newcomer had actually been here for a year, and stewing white fungus, lotus seed soup, and bird's nest porridge for the master had become a regular routine. So she corrected her mistake and said, (Sister Aigu, the coal stove is here. Go get the dabbing water equipment).

(Dabbing water equipment)! This term made her hesitate again. Probably a washbasin. That's easy. She had one at home, but it had a few holes, which could not be repaired. She had already replaced it with fifty sheets of grass paper. The image would not fade. She went to the bedroom and found one. Naturally, it was big, smooth, and beautiful. In the same place, there was also a white porcelain one, which was very deep, large, and uneven. She didn't know what it was for. Later, an idea came to her mind, and she guessed that it was for cold water. She hurried to the kitchen and dabbed it, placed it on the table, and said to the young mistress Han, (The water is here).

Young mistress Han rolled over and pushed aside the quilt, put on her slippers, and went to the table. Seeing that the cold water and hot water were all in place, she wiped the tables, chairs, spittoons, vases, bowls, and dishes around her clean, and praised happily, (Pay attention everywhere, you can do it). Aigu was relieved and became extraordinarily energetic! She was about to tidy up the (ivory bed) with the (harmony quilt). But she saw that in the bed quilt, there was also a young master hiding. She didn't pay attention, and accidentally lifted half of the quilt head, catching a glimpse of a fleshy leg. She quickly let go. The young master had already noticed it, turned around, opened his eyes, looked at her a few times, and smiled slightly. For some reason, Aigu felt like she had been electrocuted, lost her senses, and later felt that she was standing in front of a man's bed. It was very embarrassing. She hurried away, like watching the young mistress washing her face, probably not noticing. She felt relieved. But she always felt a little strange about the young master. It was (fear), not (shame), or something else. In short, she had three points of (prevention).

Commercial News

Financial Gold Market in Calm 216

Rising Three Taels and One Mace　　Yesterday's market was calm with little change. The daily high and low prices differed by no more than three taels. The final result was a rise of three taels and one mace compared to the previous day. Market sentiment was still good, with buying and selling from various parties. Except for the Guangdong group's overall selling, the remaining transactions were not large. The price rose from the early morning, mainly because the price of silver bars rose very slightly, and the silver price did not move. Later, it only fluctuated by a little over one tael, probably because the foreign exchange rate was tightening. However, Hengxing's selling intention was still strong, which hindered the price from advancing. The market was firm at first but then declined, as the U.S. dollar strengthened and then leveled off. However, the overall situation was peaceful, with fluctuations of no more than a little over one tael. Finally, it stood at around forty-seven taels. The November contract was transferred from the short seller Huiyuan to Dafeng Heng in dozens of lots, with a discount of one tael and eight mace. The detailed situation of the market before and after is recorded below.

Opening Up Three Taels and Eight Mace　　In the early morning, the December contract opened up three taels and eight mace to seven hundred and forty-seven taels and five mace. This was mainly because the silver price had not risen as expected yesterday, and the exchange rate was also more than one point higher. Hengxing sold off, and the East Asia Bank sold U.S. dollars for January at 30 yuan, and Banque Belge sold February at 0.0625. It had already fallen to forty-six taels and three mace, but within ten minutes, it rebounded by a few mace. Subsequently, buyers were eager, such as Zhaofeng Chang, Hengyu, Daxing Yong, Tianfeng Yong, Yuanxing Yong, Futaixing, Hengfu Chang, Yifeng Yong, etc. Hengxing also bought in dozens of lots, because the limit price was not easy to obtain, especially as the January U.S. dollar was strong. Andar absorbed 0.9375, and HSBC absorbed 0.675 for this month, so the price jumped by more than two taels, reaching forty-eight taels and eight mace at 9:30. The British pound was quoted at a discount of 0.125, and the U.S. dollar at 0.25. Marked Flour Discovers a Huge Decline 227

Yesterday after the opening of the flour market in the morning and afternoon, the prices of each month saw a huge decline again. The volume of transactions throughout the day was the highest of the year, and the price decline was also the smallest record since there was a stock exchange. The January price fell to 1 tael, 6 qian, 7 fen, 7 li and a half in the afternoon. As for the reason for the heavy decline, it is no more than being agitated by the world's trend, and the decline in prices has no national boundaries. The price this month was still stable at the beginning, but Fufeng, in view of the fact that most of the Tianjin flour sales have been captured by the flour, and if the current flour in this city is further increased, I am afraid that there will be no room for the sale of Shen flour in North China, so it was heard in the morning that 30,000 to 40,000 books would be thrown out, and then the building would be taken over in the afternoon. This attitude, in accordance with the world's prices, is really appropriate, because if it is not the case, it will not be possible to stop the influx of foreign flour into China. As for the distant, the quoted price of foreign wheat is still small at three to four jiao, and it can be seen that the foreign wheat market has not yet escaped from the state of oversupply. Australian wheat sales are still endless, so wheat heads are especially panic, or even because of the pursuit of evidence, it must be finished, so the selling atmosphere is very crazy, which has created a tragic decline. After this new minimum record has been seen, according to the world's prices as a ratio, I am afraid that it will still be difficult to enter a peaceful path. As a result, the price this month fell sharply by four fen compared to the previous day, December fell by four and a half fen, January fell by four fen, February fell by three and a half fen, and March and April fell by two fen and seven li and a half, it is said.

Sichuan Silk Supply Difficulties 232

The political strife in Sichuan Province is intense, and the war between the two Lius has already begun. Shipping is difficult, and the supply of Sichuan silk has been cut off. In order to maintain silk sales to Europe and America, silk merchants in the producing areas are now converting factory supplies, etc., into postal packages and delivering them to the post office for delivery. Although Sichuan silk is currently being shipped to Shanghai, the amount is almost zero. In the latter half of last month, only 175 packages were shipped. The source is still difficult to obtain in the future.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Speech

Talking About Skinning 260

— Buddha

丨Three Arts of Dealing with the World丨

The term "skinning" is not found in the classics. In common usage, it roughly means "stingy and unlucky" or "nitpicking." If a person is stingy and unlucky, no matter how prosperous their financial resources may be, they cannot manage a large business. Fan Chou of the Han Dynasty once prepared a feast for the people of the state, but by midday, the food was not available, and more than ten people left on their own. Such people are called skinners. It can be seen that skinners cannot achieve great things.

Counting the big things and not counting the small things cannot be called skinning. Not counting the big things and messing up the small things is skinning. Counting the big things and counting the small things is even more skinning.

Assuming one is frugal with oneself but generous to others, one cannot be considered a skinner. If one is not frugal with oneself but is stingy to others, that is skinning. If one is stingy with oneself and stingy with others, that is even more skinning.

Therefore, skinners are not well-liked. In my hometown, there is an old woman, over seventy years old, with no children. Her assets are no less than three or four hundred thousand gold, yet she still takes on the work of sweeping and cleaning herself, only hiring one maid. People say to her, "Madam, you are so wealthy, why do you make yourself suffer so? Why not be more lenient?" The old woman replied, "You people are lenient, so you have nothing. I am not lenient, so I have this." When the old woman died, her relatives fought over the property, even resorting to lawsuits. It can be seen that skinners are born with a hard life. Even if they have property, it is only for guarding it for others.

Now, when the problem of livelihood is becoming increasingly difficult and the standard of living is rising day by day, it is naturally wrong not to know how to be frugal and to be extravagant and dissolute. Not knowing how to be frugal is different from skinning. Frugality is saving oneself, while skinning is also scraping others. Skinning is also different from stinginess. Stinginess is being petty and unwilling to give to others. Skinning is harming others solely to benefit oneself.

However, although skinning is different from frugality, not being frugal when one should be is skinning. Although skinning is different from stinginess, being stingy when one should not be is also skinning. Therefore, having moderation in eating and drinking, using money with measure, being in what kind of situation, using what kind of display, being in what kind of position, using what kind of economy, exceeding these is mostly skinning.

Therefore, Confucius said, "Acting out of self-interest leads to much resentment."

Science

Common Misconceptions About Biology 262

— Xiaoguang

"Not knowing one thing is the shame of a Confucian scholar." In the current era where all kinds of knowledge are divided and specialized, this saying has lost its accuracy. However, common sense about ordinary natural phenomena is something everyone should know. Among natural phenomena, those most closely related to humans are biological phenomena. The general public's views on biology are often seemingly correct but actually wrong. This article aims to point out and explain a few such simple facts, hoping that readers will use this as a starting point for more in-depth and comprehensive research!

(1) Decayed Grass Turns into Fireflies

On summer nights, fireflies twinkle and dance among the flowers and grass, like countless active pearls adorning the night. Sometimes they float to the courtyard, hesitate in the room, looking around, which is quite helpful to the viewing and comforting the loneliness. How do fireflies come about? Not many people know. The "Book of Rites, Monthly Orders" says: "In the third month of summer, decayed grass transforms into fireflies." The "Materia Medica" by Tao Hongjing notes: "Fireflies are transformed from decayed grass and rotten bamboo roots." This is also an error of observation! Fireflies mostly lay eggs on the roots of grass by the water. The eggs are extremely tiny and also emit a faint light. After several metamorphoses, they become flying insects. The ancients saw fireflies appearing on decayed grass and mistakenly believed that the decayed grass had transformed into them!

(2) Earthworms Sing

At dusk, by the banks of rivers and streams, sometimes a clear, faint, and drawn-out sound is heard. The general public believes that this is emitted by earthworms. Therefore, there are folk tales such as "Earthworms sing mountain songs" and "Earthworms play the flute while frogs beat the drum." However, upon close examination of the earthworm's body, there is no sound-producing organ at all. So, who is the originator of this sound? Biologists have already determined that it is the mole cricket. The mole cricket, commonly known as the "soil dog," has a body about an inch long, is brown in color, has two pairs of wings, and strong forelimbs that are good at digging. It is attracted to lights, so it often flies into rooms. It can harm the roots of plants, making it a type of pest. The male insects vibrate their wings to make a sound in the dusk of early summer to attract female insects.

(3) Geckos are Poisonous

Geckos, commonly known as "wall lizards," belong to the lizard family. Their tails are quite brittle and can regenerate when broken off. Each limb has five toes, and the underside of the toes has a wrinkled fold that acts like a suction cup, allowing them to climb freely on walls and smooth glass windows. They feed on insects, making them beneficial animals. It is rumored that their mouths contain potent poison, but this is not true. The poisonous one is another type of scorpion, belonging to the spider family. Their bodies are about three inches long, blue-black in color, and have four pairs of legs on the thorax. The mandibles are developed like crab claws, and the abdomen has segments. The rear end is narrow and long like a tail, with a poisonous hook at the end that can sting people. These animals mostly live in warm and hot regions, are viviparous, and do not undergo metamorphosis. They hide under pebbles, wall corners, tree bark, and dead leaves during the day and come out at night to prey on insects.

(4) Cuckoos Weep Blood

Every spring and early summer, when wheat ripens and mulberries ripen, when fragrant grass is lush and green shade fills the fields, the cuckoos in the deep forests occasionally emit a sad and melancholic cry, seeming to say, "Better to return home!" Repeatedly and lingeringly, it touches people's sorrows! There is a saying that they weep blood:

"The cuckoo cries bitterly and weeps blood incessantly."!! Biya

"Weeping all night until dawn, blood stains the grass and trees."!! Avian Classics

Therefore, men of letters and poets always use the cuckoo to describe sad and sorrowful things, truly beyond enumeration. This misconception of weeping blood actually originates from imprecise observation. Originally, the cuckoo's mouth is bright red. Li Shizhen's "Compendium of Materia Medica" also states: "Shaped like a sparrowhawk but with a dark and gloomy color, with a red mouth." Even when captured cuckoos occasionally have traces of blood on their beaks, it must be due to injury. It is wrong to think that all cuckoos weep blood when they cry!

(5) Dragonflies Lay Eggs and Turn into Fish

"Butterflies fluttering through flowers are deeply seen, dragonflies skimming over water fly gently." — Du Fu

Why do dragonflies skim over water and fly? Because they lay eggs in the water. Small fish appear in the laying area later, and those who do not observe carefully mistakenly believe that these small fish are transformed from the dragonfly's eggs. Little do they know that small fish are transformed from fish eggs, and dragonfly eggs will only turn into dragonflies and will never turn into small fish!

(6) Snakes Have Feet

Everyone knows that "drawing a snake and adding feet" is wrong, but on the other hand, some people say that snakes have feet and that seeing a snake's foot will bring bad luck. This is due to imprecise observation and conjecture. Snakes move entirely by the combined action of their ribs and scales, using the scales on their abdomens to touch the ground obliquely to prevent them from sliding backward, while simultaneously curving their bodies left and right to move forward.

Social Improvement Discussion Group

Is Teasing the Newlyweds a Bad Habit? 263

— Wenbing

Humans are emotional and excitable animals, which is at least partially true. Because of this, human life is particularly rich and meaningful. Throughout the year, when festivals arrive, people gather to eat, drink, talk, and laugh, and play with lion lanterns and community theatre. When society and the country have new achievements, people also gather to celebrate. Moreover, as society evolves, the complexities and rituals of human life become even greater. Marriage is a major event in the course of one's life.

Page 21

A significant event, how can we not celebrate it! Teasing the newlyweds! This is originally a good thing to start the life of two genders, and it is also a wonderful way to enhance the feelings of family members. Not only is there no need to criticize it, but it is also necessary to promote it. Therefore, after reading Mr. Xiaoxue's "Abolish the Bad Habit of Teasing the Newlyweds," I feel that there is a need to make some clarifications.

Xiaojun said: "Teasing the newlyweds is to increase the feelings of the bride and groom, which is why there is such a move. We know that previous marriages were like a sale, ... so they came up with the wonderful method of teasing the newlyweds to enhance their feelings." I think the point of enhancing feelings is correct, but its origin is not the old-fashioned marriage of buying and selling. It also said: "...If the little couple is in pain that everyone's appearance is not suitable, and their tempers are not bitter, then you don't need to tease them, and they will be fine. On the contrary, it will only get worse and worse." This makes me dare not agree. I think the old-fashioned marriage with bitter appearances and tempers should of course be teased to further enhance their love. On the contrary, we should think of ingenious ways to make up and make peace, so as to make up for the sins of the old marriage. Don't we often see couples who are not harmonious, and the parents go to ask fortune tellers or go to the temple to get some "harmony water" for them to drink? That is unreasonable and should be abolished! Xiaojun also said: "Gradually, teasing the newlyweds has become a necessary move at weddings, a good opportunity for revenge... Social bad habits like this, what can be done!" As I said before, teasing the newlyweds has become a necessary move at weddings, which is a manifestation of the evolution of the times. There is no need to doubt and curse it. As for saying that it is a good opportunity for revenge, it is unavoidable to make dangerous words. I dare not admit that it is a social bad habit! The examples of A, B, and C cited by Xiaojun may be fictitious. I have never heard of such facts. It also said: "... Taking advantage of the wine, do as many unconscious actions as possible. Therefore, conflicts often occur between the groom and the guests, and lawsuits often occur... Why bother!" This may happen occasionally, but how can we fundamentally deny the existence of an event because of an occasional deviation? As for saying that lawsuits are caused by teasing the newlyweds, I have never heard of it. "Modern weddings, wooden marriages replace 'kissing' with 'Kiss' are extremely corrupt, ... the feelings are already very harmonious, why bother with this move?" I only think that changing "kissing" to "Kiss" is enslavement, and cannot be called corruption, and I also think that those who have feelings need to be more harmonious, so that men and women can obtain unlimited happiness between husband and wife. "Shanghai is a place of exchange of new trends, ... but it has not washed away these bad habits. I don't know how to explain it?" This is a question at the end of Xiaojun. It is precisely because Shanghai is more evolved than the mainland that this custom is more prosperous. It's just that there are some changes in the way of "teasing"! Improvement, changing playing the erhu to picking up Huai'e Lin, etc. Moreover, I think that in the future Shanghai, and even the entire society, there will be new patterns of teasing the newlyweds.

Street Society

On Xiafei Road 264

— Yiping

One year I was seriously ill and followed the doctor's advice to live on Xiafei Road for a long time. This place is humorous and quiet, with small trees on both sides and a flat avenue. If you lean on the window sill and look out idly, a car speeding from over there looks like it's rushing to heaven. I often lost my mind like this. In the shadow of the setting sun, young men and women holding hands embellish the scene with a lot of exotic scenery. But the city is a great collection of sins. This virgin-like Xiafei Road now presents a different kind of brilliance. Don't believe me? Let me tell you a story:

One Sunday, I was dragged to the French Park by a friend, passing by Xiafei Road. Next to a certain tram station, there stood a beautiful girl. Our eyes were naturally stunned by her. Just then, two trams drove up one after another, but she didn't get on. My friend said, "Mysterious street! You've already moved here." Sure enough, she saw us standing for too long and occasionally squinted and smiled, and then lowered her head shyly, which can be said to "exert the ability to seduce." I grabbed my friend's hand and started walking. After crossing a short crosswalk, I turned back to look at the place where she was standing, and a blue-eyed wanderer was holding her hand and walking towards us. Seeing us turn back to look at her, he showed a smug smile, as if saying: "Low-energy people!"

In China, where production is lagging behind, many self-proclaimed people are raising their heads and waiting to be fed. Although some people are shouting about women's occupations, they are nothing more than "red flower vases." This beautiful girl has fallen to this point, and we also bear a part of the responsibility! Is it just a stain on Xiafei Road?

Friends! Recognize your responsibilities and enjoy this humorous Xiafei Road:

"Bah! I'm really used to hearing these lies. People specially came to ask you to go with them because they think highly of you, but I didn't expect you to say such lies. It's really..." The classmate said to this temple, filled with anger and rushed straight into their dormitory.

It is said that the classmate surnamed Shang had already heard the sound of this classmate running up the stairs, so he hurriedly hid the letter he was writing in the drawer. But no matter what, there is no such fast skill. So he couldn't help but clap his hands and laugh, saying: "Oh! I see, what you call studying hard is specifically referring to practicing writing ××, haha! Tomorrow I will go to the school to advertise you."

In this way, the classmate surnamed Shang was so embarrassed that he turned red and could not say half a word. It is said that the classmate surnamed Shang was still carrying a book of Western history in his hand when he went out, preparing to review it in the theater.

Film Special Issue

Film Monographs

Now We Must Enter Creation Through Imitation (5) 266

— Chen Dabeih

Hoping that Chinese films can occupy a place in the global film industry competition, and that Chinese people can showcase our unique strengths in the performing arts, our most crucial first step is to completely separate the past from the future, dividing them into two distinct periods.

The past decade or more has been a period of imitation in our film and drama history. From today onwards, the future will be our period of originality.

In America, many "Oriental obsessed" critics compliment us as the originators of shadow plays. Consequently, a group of boastful overseas Chinese become complacent and proud. Indeed, "Luanzhou Shadow Plays" and similar forms of entertainment are still prevalent in our northern provinces and were invented before various European and American shadow plays. However, would we dare to hold up these colorful human and animal carvings made of animal hide and boast to people around the world who are fascinated by the art of film that the Chinese nation is the original inventor of shadow plays? Complimenting us as the originators of shadow plays is merely a gesture of politeness, but we cannot take undue credit and insist that this art form of the silver screen, which will eventually replace blackboards, is a distant relative of our "Luanzhou Shadow Plays." When we examine the history of film development, we see the arduous and courageous contributions of researchers in America and other Western countries to this art form, and we cannot help but feel ashamed of ourselves. Why is it that the Chinese people, who were able to invent "Leather Puppet Shadow Plays," have only stagnated and remained unchanged for centuries? Why did we not evolve "Leather Puppet Shadow Plays" into modern films ourselves? We should be ashamed, not boastful!

What "Oriental Jack Coogan," what "Chinese Lillian Gish," what "Chinese Charlie Chaplin"—titles like these were commonly seen in advertisements, promotional reviews, or news reports. We didn't feel any shame in them because we considered ourselves to be in an enlightenment period. Imitation is inevitable during the enlightenment period. Therefore, we can frankly say that the Chinese film industry before today has been entirely in a period of imitation.

National News

Recent News on the "Shanghai Express" Negotiations 267

— Zhisheng

After foreign films are imported and Chinese films are produced, they must first be sent to the Film Censorship Committee, jointly formed by the Ministry of Interior and the Ministry of Education, for review. Only after the committee approves and issues a performance license can they be publicly shown in cinemas across the country. The committee has been established for nearly two years, and both Chinese and foreign film merchants have been able to abide by the regulations and apply for censorship. Recently, due to the Paramount Pictures production, "Shanghai Express," which has been shown in various European countries and contains content that insults the Chinese people, a protest was lodged with Paramount Pictures, demanding that the film be voluntarily withdrawn and destroyed within two months. According to reports from the embassy stationed here, the film is still being shown in European cities. After a meeting on November 1st, the committee decided to notify Paramount Pictures in Shanghai and request a response, as the two-month deadline has passed. If a satisfactory response is not received, the committee will suspend the censorship of its films and request the embassy in Belgium to report whether the film is still being shown in Europe.

Foreign Article Compilation

On the Trends of Soviet Films in the Last Fifteen Years (Continued) 276

— Shi Yi

丨Based on the opinions of Harry An Potamkin丨

Because there is no difference in the selection of materials for films now compared to the past, in today's Soviet drama, there are works like "Road to Life" (this film was once shown at Ping An Theater in Tianjin, translated as "Minsheng Road," but it was said that some parts were cut), and in the past, there were also works like "Children of the Desert." Similarly, today there is "Siberian Sentinels," and in the past, there were "Red Pathisans" and "Red Gas," two works that are similar in terms of material selection. These works all depict the self-armament of workers, peasants, and soldiers to drive out all invaders who touch the Soviet Union. During this period, all films, although there are no changes in the selection of materials compared to the past, have completely abandoned the immature state of the past. This difference is significant. In the past films, all we saw were just acting actors, but now they have been replaced by the characteristics of real life. In the past, Eisenstein and Pudovkin were merely rhetoricians of "great" films, but now they have indeed intimately contacted "greatness." The syllogistic style that leads from petty bourgeois individualism (the expansion of actors) to an inhuman film performance has been declared a dead relic. In its place, what we see is the flowering of collectivism and the activity of human character in "Road to Life" and "Golden Mountain." (To be continued)
